Local News

Wang Jingwei Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning and Returned to Beijing in the Evening to Seek Medical Treatment for Chronic Illness and Issue a Written Statement

Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, arrived in Shanghai from Beijing at 7:00 AM yesterday, accompanied by Zeng Zhongming, the Vice Minister of Railways, to seek medical treatment from German doctor Noll for his chronic illness. He returned to Beijing on the night train at 11:00 PM. At 6:00 PM yesterday afternoon, Wang issued a written statement regarding the resolutions of the Central Political Conference last Wednesday on the impeachment case by the Control Yuan and the issue of Hu Hanmin going abroad, making some statements. The details are recorded as follows.

Arrived in Shanghai Yesterday Morning for Medical Treatment

Wang Jingwei, the President of the Executive Yuan, has suffered from diabetes for several years. He occasionally takes time off from Beijing to come to Shanghai for medical treatment. He arrived in Shanghai from Beijing on the night train at 7:00 AM yesterday, accompanied by Zeng Zhongming, the Vice Minister of Railways. He got off the train at Nanxiang Station, took his own car and went directly to his private residence on West Pubishi Road to rest. At around 8:00 AM, he telegraphed Dr. Noll to go and examine his old illness. He left after about an hour. According to those around him, Wang came here to treat his old diabetes, with no other tasks, and plans to return to Beijing on the night train.

Proposal by Standing Committee Members of the Central Political Conference

Wang issued a written statement yesterday afternoon, the original text of which is as follows: (Reporter asked) There are three resolutions of the Central Political Conference last Wednesday regarding the impeachment case by the Control Yuan. What are the reasons? (Wang replied) This is a proposal by five members of the Central Standing Committee, Ju Zheng, Ye Chucang, Chiang Kai-shek, Chen Guofu, and Wang Zhaoming, which was passed by the conference. Originally, the so-called separation of powers is not individual separation, without any connection. This principle is understood by scholars who have studied constitutional law. The Outline of National Reconstruction stipulates that the presidents of the five Yuan are appointed and supervised by the President during the initial period of constitutional government, which shows that although the five powers are separated, they still have a system. The current Organic Law of the National Government stipulates that the Chairman of the National Government does not bear actual political responsibility, and Article 15 stipulates that before the promulgation of the Constitution, the presidents of the five Yuan are each responsible to the Central Executive Committee of the Chinese Kuomintang, which shows that although the five powers are separated, they still have a system. The so-called Central Executive Committee, in addition to the plenary meeting held once every six months, usually has the Central Executive Committee Standing Committee to handle party affairs and the Central Executive Committee Political Conference to handle political affairs, both of which are held once a week. Currently, except for Dai Jitao, the President of the Examination Yuan, Sun Zhesheng, the President of the Legislative Yuan, Ju Juesheng, the President of the Judicial Yuan, Yu Youren, the President of the Control Yuan, and I, are all standing committee members of the Central Standing Committee and the Central Political Conference. Regarding the affairs of the five Yuan, they are responsible to the Central Executive Committee on the one hand, and seek communication and liaison within the Central Executive Committee on the other hand. Therefore, all major affairs of the five Yuan must be submitted to the Central Political Conference for approval. We only need to look at what is discussed and approved by each Central Political Conference, most of which are proposals from the Executive Yuan and the Legislative Yuan, to understand. Therefore, this time the Central Political Conference provides guidance and supervision on the affairs of the Control Yuan, just as it provides guidance and supervision on the administrative affairs of the Legislative Yuan. Some people outside believe that this resolution hinders the independence of the power of supervision, which is absolutely wrong.

Establishment of Impeachment Case by Control Yuan

The establishment of an impeachment case by the Control Yuan begins with a proposal by one member and ends with a review by three members. From this, it can be seen that the so-called establishment of an impeachment case is only the intention of the impeachment party, and the intention of the impeached party has not yet been expressed, and the intention of the disciplinary agency has not been expressed. Most people believe that the establishment of an impeachment case means that the guilt of the impeached party is established, which is an absolute misunderstanding. After the establishment of the impeachment case, the president of the Control Yuan transfers it to the disciplinary agency. If it is a general civil servant, the disciplinary agency is the Civil Servant Disciplinary Committee organized by the Judicial Yuan. If it is a political official, the disciplinary agency is the Political Official Disciplinary Committee organized by the National Government. This is the current system. According to this system, after receiving the impeachment case from the Control Yuan, the disciplinary agency notifies the impeached person within a certain period to allow them to defend themselves. After receiving the impeached person's statement, it convenes a meeting to review it, two or three times. After the review, it either judges that it should be subject to disciplinary action, or judges that it should not be subject to disciplinary action. To give an analogy, the Control Yuan is like an ordinary criminal prosecutor, and the Disciplinary Committee is like a judge. If the establishment of an impeachment case is considered the establishment of the guilt of the impeached party, it is like taking the words of the prosecutor as the crime of the impeached party, without the need for further trial, which is equally confused.

Inappropriate to Announce Before Disciplinary Action

The above is a brief explanation of the current system. The following is the origin of the resolution of the Central Political Conference. Originally, according to the Control Yuan's impeachment law, the content of all impeachment cases must not be announced before they are transferred to the disciplinary agency. As a result, many members of the Control Yuan announced the content arbitrarily to the outside world after transferring it to the disciplinary agency, and even published the full text of the impeachment case in the newspaper. It should be known that this impeachment case has only been transferred to the disciplinary agency and has not yet been notified by the disciplinary agency to the impeached person to allow them to defend themselves, let alone the review by the disciplinary agency. If the full text of the impeachment case is published at this time, isn't it only the opinion of the impeachment party, and not the opinion of the impeached party and the disciplinary agency? Is this fair? It should be known that national legislation emphasizes both rewarding good and punishing evil. For example, punishing corruption should be given equal weight to protecting integrity, and punishing those who neglect their duties and violate the law should be given equal weight to protecting those who are diligent and law-abiding. Public opinion should also be like this. Whenever an impeachment case is seen, it should not be used as a means of celebrating the punishment of the guilty. At the same time, special attention should be paid to protecting the innocent. Otherwise, how can the country and society encourage people to do good? For example, a small civil servant is impeached by a member of the Control Yuan, and after review by three members, he is accused of corruption. At the time of transferring it to the disciplinary agency, he also divulges it to the outside world. Then, everyone who reads the newspaper will recognize him as corrupt. If this civil servant receives this charge of corruption and the situation is true and the crime is confirmed, it is still acceptable. But what if he is wrongly accused? Before receiving the notice from the disciplinary agency, there is no way to defend himself. What an injustice! Even if he receives the notice from the disciplinary agency and submits a statement of defense, what ability does this small civil servant have to make this statement of defense be publicized in the newspaper in the same way as the impeachment case? Then, this civil servant's guilt was originally established after the judgment of the disciplinary agency, but now, when the impeachment case is announced, his guilt has already become known to the public in the newspaper. What an unfairness! The above is the case of a civil servant who is wrongly accused. As for political officials, it is even different. Originally, political officials bear political responsibility. Therefore, the disciplinary law does not have any punishments for political officials such as demerit, salary reduction, demotion, etc., only a reprimand for minor offenses and dismissal for serious offenses. Reprimand need not be discussed. If a political official's policy does not work, he should retire, without the need for any disciplinary action. The impact of the Control Yuan's impeachment of a political official is not only on the political official himself, but on the policy being implemented. This policy sometimes needs to be kept secret and cannot be discussed publicly. It should be known that this is not to keep it secret for the political official's own good or bad, but for the political official to keep it secret for the benefit of the country. Therefore, it is impossible for this political official, who bears political responsibility, to confront the Control Yuan's impeachment case and publish it in the newspaper. It goes without saying for national defense and foreign affairs, but other ministries and commissions sometimes need to keep secrets in the interest of national policy. In this case, it is most unfair to only allow the Control Yuan to announce the impeachment case and not allow the impeached person to announce the statement of defense. It seems fairer to announce both, but civil servants suffer from the inability to announce, and political officials suffer from the inability to announce.

Hu to Go Abroad to Promote Policies

(Asked) There are rumors that Mr. Hu Zhantang intends to go abroad. I wonder if this is true. (Answered) Mr. Hu Zhantang has indeed asked someone to indicate that he wants to go to Europe and the United States to promote policies for the central government. The colleagues of the central government have gladly agreed to this. However, because Mr. Hu has been far away in Hong Kong for several years, there must be many things about the central government's policies that he does not fully understand. We hope that Mr. Hu can come to Nanjing before traveling, or at least come to Shanghai, so that we can discuss in detail. We are now seeking Mr. Hu's consent to this proposal, but have not yet received a reply. As for whether Mr. Sun Zhesheng or Mr. Kong Yongzhi will go to Hong Kong in the future, it has not yet been decided, because Mr. Sun is on vacation in Honolulu, and Mr. Kong has just returned from North China, and there are many things to deal with, so they may not be able to leave for a while.

China-British Construction Bank Group Agrees to Lend Huge Sum to Ministry of Railways 16 Million Yuan Shared Equally Loan to Complete Gate-Cao Section and Repay Internal and External Debts

The Ministry of Railways, in order to complete the road line and bridges between Xixing and Cao'e on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway, and to repay the internal and external debts of the road, borrowed 16 million yuan from a bank group jointly formed by the China-British Bank and the China Construction Bank, and was approved to issue bonds by the bank group. Now, according to a reporter from Xin Sheng News Agency, the details are recorded as follows.

Proceeding with the Loan

The track between Xixing and Cao'e on the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway has not been built due to the Qiantang River Railway Bridge problem. The total length of the road line is 78 kilometers. As for the Cao'e River Bridge, except for the bridge foundation which has been filled, the rest was suspended due to the European War. Now the Qiantang River Railway Bridge will begin construction. The Ministry of Railways, in order to complete the section and the Cao'e River Bridge, as well as to repay the internal and external debts of the road, is proceeding to borrow money from the banking sector.

Principles Determined

In light of the fact that both the Shanghai-Nanjing and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways have been repaying their debts and interest on schedule, resulting in a daily increase in the price of bonds abroad, the British and Chinese Corporation is extremely willing to lend money to the two railways to complete the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line. At the same time, the newly opened China Development Finance Corporation is also willing to invest in the completion of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line. The Ministry of Railways dispatched personnel to join the two railway administrations to discuss loan methods with the British and Chinese Corporation and the China Development Finance Corporation. The principles have been determined.

Joint Syndicate

The total loan amount from the Ministry of Railways to the British and Chinese Corporation and the China Development Finance Corporation is 16 million yuan, which will be borrowed by a syndicate jointly organized by the British and Chinese Corporation and the China Development Finance Corporation, with 8 million yuan from the British and Chinese Corporation and 8 million yuan from the China Development Finance Corporation. The syndicate is also allowed to issue bonds that can be circulated in domestic and foreign markets. All loan terms are still under negotiation, but the interest rate is reportedly 6%.

Joint Bridge and Road Construction

The Ministry of Railways, the Zhejiang Provincial Government, and other agencies believe that the construction of the Qiantang River Railway Bridge and the completion of the Xixing to Cao'e section of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway are closely related. Now that the funds for the construction of the Qiantang River Railway Bridge have been raised, and the lending principles for the completion of the Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line have also been determined, it is rumored that a joint construction will be decided in the future, so that the entire Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo line will be connected in one go.

Representatives of the Industrial Federation to First Meet Kong in Shanghai

To Present the Advantages and Disadvantages of Not Modifying the New Tariff

According to the New Voice News Agency, the Chinese General Chamber of Industry, in response to members' requests, convened an emergency meeting on the 7th of this month at its meeting hall on Hankou Road to discuss the new import tariff announced by the Ministry of Finance. It was resolved to send representatives, including Guo Shun and six others, to petition in Beijing on a scheduled basis. The representatives were originally scheduled to depart last night, but since Minister of Finance Kong Xiangxi has not yet returned to Beijing since his return to Shanghai, the representatives intend to first present the advantages and disadvantages of not modifying the new tariff to Minister Kong in Shanghai, request his consideration, and then proceed to Beijing to petition the Executive Yuan, Legislative Yuan, Ministry of Industry, and other relevant Yuan and Ministries, hoping for remedial measures.

After Revision of the American Cotton Loan Contract, the First Batch Arrives in Shanghai Today, Totaling More Than 20,800 Pieces, Discharged at China Merchants Bureau's Chinese Warehouse

The cotton purchased by our country from the United States with loan funds will, after the contract is revised, immediately have a large batch of 10 million US dollars' worth of cotton shipped from North America to China starting in June. The first shipment was chartered by the American firm Fook Lai & Co. using the giant ship Fernlane, which was loaded with cotton at the New York United Port in North America, totaling 20,809 bales, occupying more than 10,000 tons. It was originally scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on July 15th, but due to encountering wind and fog en route, the voyage was slightly delayed, and the arrival date was two days later than originally planned. It arrived yesterday noon. A wireless message was received from the ship stating that it would be allowed to enter Wusong at noon today. Fook Lai & Co. has already hired a pilot and prepared to guide it to Shanghai, and notified the China Merchants Bureau to prepare for storage. The Bureau originally planned to store the goods in the Yangtze Wharf warehouse, but because the entire batch of cotton would be shipped one after another, totaling more than 200,000 pieces, the Yangtze Wharf alone would not be able to accommodate it, and the repair work had not yet been completed, so the first shipment arriving today was changed to be stored in the Chinese warehouse in Pudong. Yesterday, the wharf management office notified the warehouse to prepare all loading and unloading procedures. As for the cotton carried by the remaining ships, they will also be shipped to Shanghai in this short period of time. In the future, there will be 40,000 to 50,000 pieces arriving in Shanghai every month. It is also heard that three wheat ships that were blocked in the United States due to the strike have now departed from the United States and are expected to arrive in Shanghai within this week.

Site of the Central Machinery Factory Requested to Be Located in the City Center, The Seventh District Party Department Specially Submits to the City Party Department to Request the Ministry of Industry Not to Establish It in the Concession

According to the Central News Agency, the Ministry of Industry plans to establish a central machinery factory in Shanghai and has already surveyed the area around North Suzhou Road as the factory site, as reported in the previous newspaper. The Party Department of the Seventh District of this city believes that the Ministry of Industry should select the central area of this city as the factory site for the establishment of the central machinery factory. Yesterday, it specially submitted to the City Party Department to request the Ministry of Industry to re-determine the factory site. The original text stated that the Ministry of Industry originally planned to establish the central machinery factory in the capital, but now that Shanghai is the center of industry and commerce, the area around North Suzhou Road in Shanghai has been changed, etc. It is found that the central area of Shanghai is currently actively developing and the results are considerable. In the future, the center of industry and commerce will naturally be the central area of the city. Now that the Ministry of Industry has established the central machinery factory, and the factory site is sheltered in the concession, it seems to contradict the Prime Minister's plan to open up a greater Shanghai port. For this reason, it is proposed to submit a document to your department to request the Ministry of Industry to determine the factory site of the central machinery factory in the central area of the city, in order to seek the prosperity of a greater Shanghai, which is truly a public convenience.

Fire Brigades in Various Districts Carry Out Drought Prevention Work, Dispatched Ten Pump Trucks, Set Off to Rural Areas to Pump Water, Conducted in Nine Districts

According to the National News Agency, the City Government of this city, considering that the rural areas in the city are facing a drought due to the long-term drought, has convened the 264th meeting of the government and decided to allocate 60,000 yuan to purchase a large number of water pumps and distribute them to various rural areas for application, which will be entirely handled by the Social, Land, and Public Security Bureaus, etc. However, since the water pumps could not be rushed for a while, Wen Hongen, the director of the Public Security Bureau, instructed Dong Zhihe, the director of the fire protection section of the second section of the bureau, to order ten fire pump trucks from the fire brigades in various districts of this city to go to various rural areas to pump water, which was conducted in nine districts: (1) "Longhua District" was the responsibility of the Shanghai North and South District fire brigades; (2) "Pengpu District" was handled by the third section of the Zhabei fire brigade; (3) "Zhabei District" was the responsibility of the fourth section of the Zhabei fire brigade; (4) "Caojing District" was handled by the Shanghai South and West District fire brigades; (5) "Pusong District" was jointly conducted by the Caoxi Road in Western Shanghai and the Dongjiadu fire brigades in Southern Shanghai; (6) "Yinxiang District" was the responsibility of the first section of the Zhabei fire brigade; (7) "Yinhang District" was the responsibility of the second section of the Zhabei fire brigade; (8) "Jiangwan District" was handled by the Jiangwan fire brigade; (9) "Zhenru District" was the responsibility of the Zhenru Town fire brigade. At 9:00 am yesterday, Director Dong of the bureau went to Yishiyuan on Ninghe Road to contact the drought relief committee and worked with representatives from various rural areas to handle the matter. Therefore, the fire brigades in various districts have set off to conduct the work since 10:00 am yesterday.

In the Zhabei District, the Fire Brigade Union convened various fire brigades the day before yesterday to discuss relief distribution methods. It was designated that in addition to the third section responsible for the Pengpu District and the fourth section responsible for the Yinxiang District, which have already been mobilized, the first and second sections in the territory, due to the relatively frequent fires, will take care of the Zhabei District in the vicinity for the sake of local consideration. It is heard that since yesterday (the 16th), the respective sections have dispatched vehicles to work with the farmers' association to start pumping water at the Baziqiao on Liuyin Road in Zhabei to facilitate irrigation and provide temporary relief.

Rice Price Increases Due to Drought Hindering Transportation, City Government Orders Cease, Abundant Stock in the Interior, Foreign Merchants Purchasing Foreign Rice

According to the Central News Agency, the city government, in addition to allocating funds for drought relief, considers the soaring rice prices in the market to have a significant impact on the people's food and has ordered the city's Social Affairs Bureau to investigate the matter. It has been found that the rice price in this city has soared due to the long-term drought, and has increased by more than three yuan per stone in less than half a month. If it continues to increase, it will inevitably affect the people's food. The government previously approved the Zhejiang Provincial Government's telegram requesting restrictions on rice prices, and ordered the bureau to comply. It is hereby ordered again that the bureau immediately comply and promptly and properly stop any opportunistic profiteering to maintain the people's food and calm the people's hearts, and report the handling situation. This order is issued. It is now known that the City Social Affairs Bureau has been ordered to inform the rice merchants to restrict rice prices to maintain the people's food.

According to Jiang Shizhi, the chairman of the Rice Grain Guild, the rice and grain in Shanghai are supplied by Wuxi, Changshu, Suzhou, Jiaxing, Songjiang, Jiashan, Qingpu, Jiangyin, Changzhou, Yixing, Liyang, and other places. Because all places have had good harvests in the past three years, the grain stock in the interior is more than in previous years. According to the statistics obtained at the end of the abolished lunar calendar's Dragon Boat Festival, the total number of grains stored in the above-mentioned places is more than 600,000 stones of japonica rice, more than 300,000 stones of indica rice, and more than 200,000 stones of glutinous rice, totaling 1.2 million stones. As of now, the total stock is still more than 700,000 stones. According to estimates, this number is sufficient to maintain the market until the new rice is available.

Reduced Arrivals

Normally, the total number of rice ships arriving in Shanghai from various places every day in the north and south markets reaches 70 (each boat can hold 100 to 200 stones of rice, averaging about 12,000 stones). Compared to the long-term drought without rain, the fields are cracked, and the river water in Jiangyin, Changzhou, Yixing, Liyang, and other places is blocked, causing rice ships to disappear. The number of rice ships in Suzhou and Changzhou has also sharply decreased. On average, only 30 ships arrive in the north and south markets every day. However, the rice stock in Shanghai can still be maintained for one or two weeks.

Reasons for Price Increase

Jiang also stated that the reasons for the gradual increase in rice prices are: (1) The small rivers in the interior have no water, and the grains from the surrounding countryside cannot be transported to the town; (2) Those who have stored rice and want to sell it are prevented by the villagers in order to prevent drought; (3) Rice merchants in this port have been going to the interior to buy large quantities of grain, and tens of thousands of stones have already been transacted; (4) People's hearts are not calm, so many are hoarding rice to wait for the famine; (5) Rice merchants are hoarding and not selling; (6) Speculators are raising prices to buy; (7) Due to the drought without rain, the farmers are mostly focused on irrigating the fields and building dams to store water, and rice ships are blocked. Due to these complex reasons, an unprecedented panic has been created.

Huge Profits

The New Voice News Agency reporter also investigated the rice transport merchants, saying that the rice stock in the interior is indeed still abundant, but most of the boat households are currently planting rice and irrigating, resulting in fewer rice ships arriving. Normally, moving rice from the interior to Shanghai can earn a profit of two to three corners to five corners per stone after expenses, which is already a great business. Now, due to the unrest in people's hearts and the manipulation of some people, each stone of rice can earn a profit of three to four yuan. The price of grain, which is more than four yuan per dan, is sold for thirteen yuan after shelling at a 50% discount, plus food expenses, wages, and interest. Therefore, the general rice transport merchants are all making three times the profit in the market and are overjoyed.

Future of People's Food

According to another source, the rice industry is considering ordering 500,000 stones of foreign rice to prevent famine. However, looking back at the flood of 1931, the ordering of foreign rice caused a sharp decline in domestic rice. If this is done again this time, domestic products will also suffer a great impact in the future. This year, the grain in Jiangbei has had a bumper harvest, as has Hunan. The situation in Jiangxi is equal in terms of good and bad harvests. Therefore, domestic rice and grain are sufficient to maintain the people's food in various places, and there is no need to panic. Ordering foreign rice is superfluous.

Foreign Merchants' Request

According to the Shanghai Times News Agency, foreign merchants engaged in importing and exporting grains in this port, such as Daofu, Anli, Xiangmao, Gongping, Taifeng, and Xinfeng, are concerned about the increasing drought and rising rice prices in our country, which show a shortage of domestic grain. They can ship and sell imported grain, but due to tariff restrictions, they must pay 1.65 gold units per 100 kilograms, which is still too burdensome and difficult to promote sales. They specially sent representatives to Beijing to request the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to reduce the tax by half. The Ministry of Foreign Affairs reported the situation to the Executive Yuan and consulted with the Ministries of Finance and Industry. The result was that the matter was related to national policy and should not be changed easily. If it is necessary to import duty-free, it should also be planned by the Executive Yuan as a whole. Within a certain quantity range, special permission should be granted for import, and foreign merchants should not use this to make profits. Therefore, the foreign merchants' request did not have any results.

Ordered One Thousand Tons

Although the foreign merchants' request did not achieve its purpose this time, they believe that the recent soaring rice prices, compared with foreign countries, are still profitable even after paying tariffs. Currently, Daofu Foreign Company has telegraphed to Saigon to order 1,000 tons to China, which will be fully sold by the major rice shops on Dou Market Street, with a transaction price of 10.1 yuan per dan. It can arrive in Shanghai soon. The bean and rice industry will also import 500,000 dan of duty-free foreign rice. The rice price in this port is expected to stabilize with the backing of foreign rice, and will not skyrocket again.

Cai Zengji Talks About Issuing City Public Bonds, Discussing Construction is Truly a Matter of Utmost Urgency, The Principal and Interest Repayment Fund is the Most Secure

According to the Central News Agency, the 3.5 million yuan of municipal bonds issued by this city in 1934 has been approved by the central government and is scheduled to be issued today. Cai Zengji, the director of the city's Finance Bureau, made the following remarks on the issuance of public bonds yesterday: "This city has to issue public bonds in order to cope with municipal facilities. Shanghai is a major port in East Asia, the center of the world market, and the hub of the nation's culture. At a time when the world is intent on construction and making rapid progress, today's Shanghai cannot be compared with Shanghai sixty years ago when it was stuck in its ways. Therefore, the responsibilities of today's Shanghai Municipal Government are extremely heavy, and all those who care about the world situation are well aware of this. According to the modern cities that concentrate culture, to solve all kinds of complex problems, it must first have considerable basic facilities. This city is an important city, so it cannot be an exception. However, looking back at this city since the revolution, most of the facilities have been lacking. The sports field, museum, library, hospital, slaughterhouse, etc., which are currently being discussed for construction, are only a part of the above-mentioned basic facilities, and are truly a matter of utmost urgency. These facilities are being gradually implemented in the special zones of this city. This city's makeshift measures are not worthy of the citizens who pay taxes, and the inferiority is also crucial to the national system. Moreover, those who plot against us often use the fact that the Chinese people lack organization and management capabilities as propaganda. If we do not strive for progress in the small matter of municipal facilities, we will not be able to correct the world's view. However, since the discussion of the above-mentioned items is so urgent, and the annual regular income of this city has designated uses, it is necessary to issue public bonds to cope with it. As for the reason for issuing public bonds, the use of foreign capital is actually beneficial and harmless. According to recent surveys, more than half of the surplus silver in Shanghai belongs to foreign merchants, mostly due to the annual international trade surplus stored in Shanghai. Under the current environment, this foreign capital is unlikely to flow into the interior. If foreign merchants do not invest in Shanghai to make profits, they will inevitably remit a large amount of cash to their home countries. For the government's sake, to stabilize domestic finance, it should try to make use of it and not allow it to overflow. Therefore, the late Prime Minister advocated the use of foreign capital, which is a clear instruction, and he has seen this. This city's issuance of public bonds will be underwritten by a Sino-foreign syndicate organized by Xinfeng Foreign Company. In the future, foreign merchants will account for the majority of those who invest in these public bonds. This city can use foreign capital to develop municipal administration, which will also be of considerable benefit to domestic finance. As for the lower interest rate of foreign capital, that is another matter. This time, the issuance of public bonds will use the car donations for cars, motorcycles, and bicycles in this city as a fund for repaying the principal and interest, which is also the most secure. The roads in this city have been expanding in recent years, and the number of vehicles has also been increasing. The annual income from the above-mentioned three car donations has reached more than 600,000 yuan. Allocating the above to the public bond's principal and interest repayment fund is truly more than sufficient. In recent years, the highways of the five provinces and cities of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Ningbo, and Shanghai have been completed, and cars can be interconnected. In the future, vehicles that donate for city licenses can reach the highways and roads of the five provinces and cities, including about 718 kilometers in Jiangsu Province, about 912 kilometers in Zhejiang Province, about 120 kilometers in Anhui Province, and about 350 kilometers in this city. All vehicles can maximize their functional use and will become more developed in the future. It can be asserted that compared to vehicles that only donate for special zone licenses and can only travel within the special zone (the roads in the two special zones total about 360 kilometers), the effect cannot be compared. In the future, vehicles in the special zones will be aware of the disparity in usage opportunities and will try to obtain city licenses as much as possible. The car donation income in this city will be even more considerable. As for the market price of this public bond, it will be registered in the Shanghai Public Industry Association after issuance and can be circulated to the foreign financial market. Its price will gradually increase. For example, the disaster area reconstruction public bonds issued last time are now more than 3% above the face value, which can be proved."

Ministry of Communications Holds, Telephone Bureau Collects Telegrams Method, Implemented Yesterday

In order to facilitate communication, the Ministry of Communications has entrusted the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau to handle all telegrams sent to the above-mentioned places, collect and send them on behalf of the Ministry in places where there are no telegram bureaus in Xiangshan, Lin'an, and other places in Zhejiang Province. It has been implemented since yesterday. The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau has received a training instruction from the Ministry of Communications to notify it. The details are as follows: The training instruction of the Ministry of Communications states that the Ministry's method of entrusting the Zhejiang Provincial Government to handle long-distance telephone calls in the Zhejiang region has been agreed upon and will be implemented from July 16 this year. According to Article 5 of the aforementioned method, telegrams to and from various places where the Ministry has not set up telegraph bureaus and various places in the country may be collected and sent on behalf of the branch bureaus of the provincial-run telephone company in each place, and a method has been formulated and issued to the Zhejiang Electric Administration for record. All branch bureaus of the Zhejiang Provincial Telephone Bureau that handle telegrams on behalf of the Bureau and their names in Romanized spelling are compiled into a list, together with the method for collecting and sending telegrams on their behalf, and issued to the Bureau. In addition to being distributed, they are to be followed.

Locations Handled: The places where telegrams are collected and sent on behalf of the Bureau include Ji'an, Huabu, Yiwu, Lin'an, Nantian, Xiangshan, Songyang, Tangqi, Tiantai, Qingtian, Tonglu, Yuhang, and Yuqian.

Collection and Delivery Methods: The methods for collecting and sending telegrams on behalf of the Bureau are: (1) This method is formulated in accordance with the provisions of Article 5 of the method of entrusting the Zhejiang Provincial Government by the Ministry of Communications to handle long-distance telephone calls. (2) Telegrams to and from various places where the Ministry has not set up telegraph bureaus and various places in the country may be collected and sent on behalf of the branch bureaus of the provincial-run long-distance telephone company in each place. Telegrams to and from foreign countries will be handled later.

Mr. Hua's Remarks: According to Hua Shijian, the director of the telegram service section of the bureau, speaking to the East China News Agency reporter, "The method of collecting and sending telegrams on behalf of the Telephone Bureau is that telegrams sent from Shanghai to the above-mentioned telegram bureaus are first sent by telegraph from Shanghai to the nearby telegram bureaus, and then the telegram bureaus notify the telephone bureaus, which record them in writing and then send them to the recipients."

海關稅務司　解釋復出口貨辦法　貨物與報單相符自可免稅放行

The Customs Commissioner of Jianghai Customs responded yesterday to the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce, stating that he had received a letter from the Ironware, Hardware, and four other industry associations, concerning the difficulty of maintaining the original form of iron goods when they are re-exported, and requesting consideration. The Commissioner stated that the association's concerns had been noted. According to the reply, these metal products may be granted the benefits of semi-bulk cargo. When re-exported, if the permit or duplicate permit is presented, detailing the imported goods and the declared goods, and the Customs inspection confirms their conformity, they may be released duty-free. The practice of cutting iron into small pieces locally remains unchanged. However, if cutting is desired locally, it must be stated on the import declaration. The treatment of materials disassembled from original ships locally is the same. However, the applicant must clearly state the approximate number of materials expected to be obtained from the ship's disassembly on the import declaration. The reply was sent for the Chamber of Commerce to note and inform the relevant parties.

These vendors often use deceptive and extortionate means to entice people to buy, causing dozens of fights and quarrels every day. If this is not strictly prohibited, it will not only hinder business but also obstruct traffic and disrupt order. Our stores are unable to tolerate such disturbances. Therefore, we jointly write to request that your federation send a letter to the police authorities to effectively stop and strictly prohibit this behavior. Accordingly, we have found that vendors congregate on Fujian Road, especially at the intersection of Zhengjia Muqiao and Avenue Edward VII, creating disturbances with their shouting, disrupting order, obstructing traffic, and hindering legitimate business. Therefore, we write to request that you promptly order your subordinates to strictly prohibit such behavior, and expel the vendors to maintain business peace and order.

小孩游泳溺斃

Liu Lingeng, an eleven-year-old child from Hebei, lived at No. 10 Andeli, Lan Road intersection, Yangshupu Road. Yesterday afternoon at about 5:00 PM, Lingeng went to the river near the Lan Road intersection to bathe because of the hot weather. However, the child did not know how to swim and lost his balance, falling into the center of the river, sinking to the bottom. When he floated up and was noticed, he had already drowned. Although he was rushed to the hospital for emergency treatment, it was ultimately ineffective. The body was then transported to the coroner's office for examination.

新民路破獲紅丸機關

Qian Baotai from Jiangbei lived at No. 1184 Xinmin Road, Zhabei, and ran a shoetree shop there. It was reported that the Public Security Bureau of the Fourth District suddenly received a tip the night before last, stating that a red pill factory was located in the house and that the pills were being sold in the area. After receiving the news, the district bureau immediately dispatched officers to search and arrest the suspects. As a result, two bags of red pills, totaling 2,000 pills, were found in the store, as well as 23 small packets, totaling over 400 pills, and four empty bags. The store owner, Qian Baotai, as well as Chen Laosi and Wang Daishi, were taken to the district bureau. After questioning, the case was deemed criminal and transferred to the Third Section of the General Bureau for investigation and handling.

無名男女屍報騐

Ji Zhukang, the security chief of the 26th Bao, 13th Tu, reported to the local court yesterday afternoon that an unidentified male corpse, approximately 20 years old, was discovered this morning in the fields near the Longhua Airfield. The upper body was naked, and the lower body was wearing white cotton trousers, light yellow socks, and striped flannel shoes. No family members were found. Therefore, he came to report the case for an autopsy. Zhao Xiangyan, the security chief of the 28th Bao, 3rd Tu, also reported to the local court that an unidentified female corpse, approximately 50 years old, was found dead this morning at the intersection of Zhoujiaqiao, Lincoln Road, and Hope Lane. A thorough search revealed no family members claiming the body. The case involved a human life and should be examined. Inspector Yang An was then appointed to lead Coroner Xuan Zhiming to inspect and seal the corpses in coffins.

公平路今晨火警　一男四女受傷

At approximately 0:14 this morning, a fire broke out at the Shun Chang Paint Shop at No. 293, Fair Road, in the Public Concession. Thick smoke made it impossible to approach. The fire spread to neighboring buildings at Nos. 295 to 297. The Eastern District Fire Brigade rushed to the scene and made every effort to extinguish the blaze, which was brought under control at 1:45 AM. Because it was the middle of the night, the residents who were caught in the fire woke up from their sleep. Upon hearing the fire alarm, they fled for their lives. As a result, one man and four women were either burned or fell from the upper floors and were sent to the Tongren Hospital and Bazilu Sanatorium by ambulance for treatment. A total of three houses were burned down.

They are all very experienced in their work. The female workers plan to stay in Shanghai for eighteen months, while the male workers plan to stay for five years. If this is successful in the future, they also plan to continue to recruit skilled workers to Shanghai. This move will have a far-reaching impact on the British cotton industry in China.

Taxpayer's Reply to the City Federation Branch: Chinese Merchant Insurance is Reliable; Jardine Matheson & Co. Seeks to Evade Compensation to the Yi Feng Factory; All Industries Should Know How to Choose Insurance in the Future

The Chinese Taxpayers' Association of the Concession received a letter from the 11th District Branch of the City Federation, requesting assistance in negotiating the delayed payment of fire insurance compensation by Jardine Matheson & Co. The Association stated that the matter concerned commerce and instructed the City Chamber of Commerce to request action, and advised that future insurance be taken out with Chinese merchant insurance companies. The original letter is recorded below:

City Federation Letter: To Whom It May Concern, we have received a letter from our member, Yi Feng Hosiery Factory, stating that our factory unfortunately suffered two accidental fires on May 20th and 21st of last year, which were both extinguished by our own efforts. Prior to the fires, we had insured with Jardine Matheson & Co. for fire insurance amounting to 26,800.08 foreign dollars, with Wing Fung Insurance for 15,000 foreign dollars, and with Si Ming Insurance for 11,000 foreign dollars. After the incidents, the three companies designated San Yi Public Assessment Firm as loss investigators. They issued a detailed loss statement, calculating the destruction at 2,351.20 foreign dollars, and the permanent loss at 907.20 foreign dollars. After reporting to San Yi Public Assessment Firm, the firm assessed the loss at 1,930 foreign dollars, which was a significant discrepancy from our factory's actual losses. Although we contested this vigorously without success, we had no choice but to reluctantly accept it. San Yi Firm then prepared a formal report and sent it to the insurance companies. Wing Fung was to pay 442.29 foreign dollars and Si Ming was to pay 402.09 foreign dollars, which we received in full on the 19th and 20th of this month. However, Jardine Matheson & Co.'s portion of 1,085.62 foreign dollars has not been formally acknowledged to date. After our factory sent a letter of inquiry, the company made excuses and procrastinated, claiming that it was still under investigation. To date, no progress has been made. Considering their intentions, it is clear that they are deliberately delaying payment, intending to evade their responsibility. If this precedent is set, our Chinese merchant policyholders will lose their protection in the future. Therefore, we are writing to request that your esteemed Association forward this letter to the Chinese Taxpayers' Association, requesting that they write to Jardine Matheson & Co. to negotiate. We hereby express our sincere gratitude for your assistance.

Taxpayers' Association Letter: In response to your letter regarding Jardine Matheson & Co.'s failure to pay insurance compensation, requesting our assistance in negotiating, we have determined that this case falls within the scope of commercial matters. Yi Feng Hosiery Factory should be advised to request the Shanghai City Chamber of Commerce to negotiate. Furthermore, Si Ming Insurance has already paid the full amount for the fire insurance taken out by Yi Feng Hosiery Factory, while Jardine Matheson & Co. is making excuses and procrastinating. This clearly demonstrates that the credibility of Chinese merchant insurance companies is indeed superior to that of foreign merchants. Rather than lamenting after the fact, it is better to carefully choose beforehand. It is our Association's intention that your esteemed Association should inform all members, based on these facts, that future insurance should be taken out with Chinese merchant companies, so that profits do not flow overseas and protection is more secure. This is our reply to the 11th District Branch of the City Federation.

This Year's Fish Market Value Plummets; Japanese Fishing Vessels Seize Opportunity to Encroach

According to the Central News Agency, the value of fish in the market has plummeted this year, according to the Municipal Fisheries Guidance Institute. Although the catch is still abundant, fishermen are still suffering. The total quantity of fish produced last month was 237,143 dan, valued at 1,287,308.53 foreign dollars. This included large yellow croaker, small yellow croaker, starry fish, shad, and other refrigerated fish. The production volume was greater than in the same month last year, but the value was lower. For example, the quantity of large yellow croaker increased by 12,403 dan compared to the same month last year, but the value decreased by 214,678.25 foreign dollars. The same applies to other fish products. As for Japanese fishing vessels, although there have been no apparent imports in the past two months, according to the institute's inquiries with fishing vessel crew members and commercial vessel drivers traveling to Shanghai, a large number of Japanese fishing vessels have been witnessed seizing our country's territorial waters and fishing rights. Furthermore, according to visitors from Shengshan, the nets and fishing lines of our country's coastal fixed-net fishing industry have been destroyed by Japanese fishing vessels rushing about. Fishermen have suffered incalculable losses, and it is said that this type of fixed-net fishing is about to disappear from the waters near Jiangsu and Zhejiang.

Gatekeeper Pursues Debt, Bites Off Mistress's Left Ear; The Inside Story is Incomplete and Untrue, Including a Blood Oath with a Severed Finger

Tao A Mao, a 37-year-old Nanjing native, works as a laborer in the Shanghai Municipal Council Engineering Department. He lives with his wife, Lin Mei, at 1219 Siwen Lane, North Gate. His wife does laundry and mending to supplement the household income. Li Yichen, a Shandong native in his thirties, is a watchman and patrolman at the Shanghai Bank's Lao Zha Bridge No. 2 warehouse. He is unmarried. Two years ago, Li became acquainted with Lin Mei when he asked her to mend his dirty clothes. Soon, Li felt his life was monotonous and was attracted to Lin Mei,

Who Possessed Some Beauty.

Li began to send her gifts and took advantage of opportunities to seduce her. Before long, Lin Mei succumbed to petty greed and was seduced by Li, becoming his mistress. Later, the two often met in hostels for secret trysts. In July of last year, Tao suddenly lost his job and was unemployed at home. He was depressed and became ill, bedridden. His wife, Lin Mei, facing a difficult economic situation at home, borrowed 40 foreign dollars from Yichen to pay for her husband's medical treatment. Before long, Tao recovered from his illness, but because he had been unemployed for a long time and had no income, he was unable to repay Li.

Unable to Repay.

Recently, Li became angry because he had repeatedly demanded repayment from Tao without success. He threatened to shoot Lin Mei's entire family. Lin Mei was frightened and, with her husband's consent, moved to 1333 San Tai Wharf Road, South City, last month to avoid Yichen. Unexpectedly, Li discovered their new location. Yesterday afternoon at around 3:00 PM, he tracked them down and confronted Tao, demanding the repayment of the debt. An argument ensued. Lin Mei, seeing the situation, intervened because Yichen had a physical relationship with her, but now he was harassing them over a mere 40 foreign dollar debt,

With No Sense of Justice.

She immediately stepped forward to defend her husband and began to fight with Li, angering him. He lunged forward, grabbed Lin Mei's head, and bit off half of her left ear with his teeth. Blood gushed out, and she screamed in pain. Nearby police officers heard the commotion and arrived, arresting Li and taking the injured Lin Mei to the First Precinct, First Station. During a preliminary hearing by Chief Yi, Tao and Lin Mei (29 years old) explained the situation, requesting a thorough investigation. Li Yichen confessed that he had an affair with Lin Mei two years ago, and the Tao family knew about it. At that time, Lin Mei insisted on divorcing her husband

To Live with Me Until Old Age.

However, for moral reasons, I refused her request. Fearing that Lin Mei suspected I had other intentions, I painfully bit off half of my left little finger in front of her and used the blood to write "Blood Oath" on a towel. I also wrote a seven-character poem in ink: "We met not long ago, our love is as heavy as a mountain. Lacking any consolation, I cut off my left finger to show my heart." This was to show her my devotion and sincerity. Afterwards, Lin Mei tricked me out of more than 300 dollars. Then, last autumn, Lin Mei borrowed another 150 foreign dollars from me and

Made a Written Agreement.

Unexpectedly, Lin Mei and I suddenly became estranged and forgot our past relationship, treating me as a stranger. Last month, Lin Mei took advantage of my absence and, with the help of several female friends, sneaked into my house and stole her IOU and the blood-stained towel. She then fled to South City with her family. But in the end, I discovered their location and came to South City today to demand repayment, leading to the conflict. He was then ordered to prepare a document and hand it over to the Municipal Public Security Bureau for investigation.

Representatives of the Cigarette and Currency Exchange Guild to Petition Today

The Shanghai Cigarette and Currency Exchange Guild is applying to register for this season's tobacco and alcohol business license tax. Yesterday, they received a letter from the South Shanghai Branch Office stating, "To Whom It May Concern: At the recent meeting of representatives of various sections of our members, it was stated that the license tax has been collected by the Municipal Finance Bureau in accordance with the Ministry's order. Merchants should fulfill their tax obligations and apply for registration in accordance with regulations. However, most of our South Shanghai businesses are small shops run by couples with few employees who are illiterate. They do not understand the registration rules and regulations. Therefore, we should request the Association to submit a petition to the Finance Bureau, requesting them to approve the petition and issue registration forms. The Association will then forward the forms to our members for completion to avoid misunderstandings. We also request that the deadline and warning period be extended by ten days beyond the original twenty days. We also request that the Municipal Chamber of Commerce forward the request to the Municipal Government for prompt approval to facilitate the process. (Omitted below)" After receiving this letter, the Association immediately convened a standing committee meeting and resolved to appoint Chen Liangyu, Shen Weiting, Zhang Songxing, Zhang Bingyuan, Chai Yasheng, Chen Kunxian and other representatives, along with representatives from various alcohol industry groups, to go to the Municipal Chamber of Commerce at 2:00 PM today to petition for the authorities to maintain the status quo and avoid increasing the burden on the tobacco and alcohol industries.

The Residents of the Eight Counties of Yangzhou are Outraged by the "Random Talk on Yangzhou" Dispute; The Association of Yangzhou Residents in Shanghai Held an Emergency Meeting Yesterday; Presented to the Central Government for Justice; Scheduled to Receive the Press

The Yangzhou Association of Residents in Shanghai, because the book "Random Talk on Yangzhou" written by Mr. Yi Junzuo, director of the Compilation and Examination Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education, and published by the Chung Hwa Book Company, contained excessive insults to the people of Yangzhou, specially organized the "Committee to Investigate the 'Random Talk on Yangzhou' Book by the Yangzhou Residents in Shanghai", and conducted negotiations with the Chung Hwa Book Company and the author Yi Junzuo. These matters have been recorded in this newspaper. The Association held a special meeting again yesterday afternoon, resolving to present the case to the central government for justice, and scheduled a meeting to receive news reporters to report everything. The details are as follows:

Emergency Meeting

The Association held an emergency special meeting at 4:00 PM yesterday at the Yangzhou Association of Residents in Shanghai. The meeting was chaired by Hou Dachun, and the following resolutions were passed: (1) Issue a statement regarding the insults to the people of Yangzhou by the Chung Hwa Book Company and the author of "Random Talk on Yangzhou," Yi Junzuo. (2) The author of "Random Talk on Yangzhou," Yi Junzuo, is currently the director of the Compilation and Examination Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education and has the power to review publications throughout Jiangsu Province. The Chung Hwa Book Company's publication of "Random Talk on Yangzhou" raises suspicions of catering to and flattering Yi Junzuo, and Yi Junzuo is suspected of abusing his authority. A telegram was sent to Yangzhou, adding a charge of dereliction of duty against Yi Junzuo, director of the Compilation and Examination Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education. (3) Resolved to hold the Second Congress of the Committee to Investigate the "Random Talk on Yangzhou" Book by the Yangzhou Residents in Shanghai at 3:00 PM on the afternoon of the 18th. (4) Telegraph to Yangzhou to send representatives to Shanghai to participate. (5) Schedule a meeting to receive the press.

Reply to Chung Hwa

The Association sent a letter to the Chung Hwa Book Company yesterday, stating, "To Whom It May Concern, we have received your letter of July 13th and acknowledge its contents. Publishers should carefully review the contents and wording of books before publishing them. Otherwise, even if the content involves criminal propaganda or reactionary works, they will be exempted from responsibility on the grounds of 'no preconceived notions'. Words involving libel and insult, publicly published, regardless of the truth or falsehood of the facts, bear the same legal responsibility. Therefore, your statement that it is not easy to judge the truth or falsehood cannot be used as a reason to evade responsibility. The fact that the book has now been discontinued is proof that its content and wording do indeed violate the law, no less than your own admission. So how can you explain the fact that you sacrificed our entire township's ethnic group as a tool for the book company to profit from? This matter is of the utmost importance to the character and reputation of our fellow townsmen. In addition to actively investigating all the responsibilities that your book company should bear, we find your reply in the letter unsatisfactory. We hereby inform you and hope you will take note.

Presentation to the Central Government

The Association telegraphed the Central Government yesterday, stating: "To the Central Party Department, the President of the Executive Yuan, the President of the Control Yuan, the Minister of the Ministry of Judicial Administration, the Minister of the Ministry of Education, the Chairman of the Jiangsu Provincial Government, and the Director of the Department of Education: Yi Junzuo's book "Random Talk on Yangzhou," printed and distributed by the Chung Hwa Book Company, and printed and sold by Lu Feikui on behalf of the Chung Hwa Book Company, contains the chapter "The Life of Yangzhou People," which is absurd in its wording. It uses frivolous language and fabricated facts to completely slander our entire ethnic group of Yangzhou, regardless of men, women, the living, the dead, and all other facilities, leaving no room. The insults to the women of Yangzhou are especially severe, and the most insane is the false claim that the entire national prostitution industry is run by women from Yangzhou, that all prostitutes are from the seven counties of Yangzhou, and that the traitors in the Shanghai war are also Yangzhou people. Yi Junzuo is currently the Director of the Compilation and Examination Department of the Jiangsu Provincial Department of Education. The book was printed by the Chung Hwa Book Company, a nationally renowned publisher of numerous textbooks, and Lu Feikui was named as the representative of the Chung Hwa Book Company. The publication period happened to be after Yi took office as the Director of Compilation and Examination. The author did not exercise caution in his position at the center of the province's culture, and the publisher abandoned its cultural propaganda position, which it had built up over decades. The hidden circumstances are unknown, but Yi Junzuo used his power and opportunity to have the book published by the Chung Hwa Book Company. The Chung Hwa Book Company, based on its inferior nature of flattering its superiors, colluded with Yi, and the matter is extremely obvious. Someone once wrote a book insulting Muslims, and the government authorities severely punished them. The circumstances of Yi Junzuo, the Chung Hwa Book Company, and Lu Feikui are even more excessive, and they dare to try again. Not only will the people of the seven counties of Yangzhou and their descendants be shamed for generations, but if this is not severely punished according to the law, it will not only cause our government's discipline to lose its effectiveness, but also cause the division of ethnic groups in various parts of the country, and the reputation of a part of the citizens of the Republic of China will be tarnished, causing a great impact. The Association, on behalf of all Yangzhou residents in Shanghai, requests that Yi Junzuo be immediately dismissed from his post, and that he and Lu Feikui be arrested and sent to court to be severely punished according to the law for public officials' crimes. The Chung Hwa Book Company should be closed down, and all original copies of "Random Talk on Yangzhou" and unsold books should be confiscated and burned, and the book should be permanently banned from being printed, sold, and circulated. Yi Junzuo, the Chung Hwa Book Company, and Lu Feikui should be ordered to compensate the entire people of the seven counties of Yangzhou for their loss of reputation. The people of Yangzhou and the Muslims are both Chinese nationals, and your ministry should treat this reasonable request equally, follow precedents, and await orders with utmost respect. The Yangzhou Association of Residents in Shanghai salutes."

Shanghai National Goods Company Offers Low Prices and High Quality; The Business is Extremely Prosperous

The Shanghai National Goods Company, located opposite the Rainbow Temple on Nanjing Road, has recently seen ladies from all walks of life flocking to buy its goods because of its low prices and high quality. Various national goods are being heavily discounted, such as printed georgette and real silk chiffon, selling for only 28 cents per foot. Heavy double crepe cheongsam fabric and Guangdong's top-grade Kao Yunsha pants fabric are selling for one dollar each. Large bath towels are selling for 50 cents per dozen, modern printed cotton fabric is selling for 50 cents per foot, Shunfeng brand lycra silk stockings are selling for 50 cents per pair, and women's cotton stockings are selling for 10 cents per pair. Thermos bottles are selling for 30 cents each, and the rest of the goods in various departments are also low-priced. The company aims to promote national goods and sells at low profit margins, which other stores cannot match. Therefore, its business is exceptionally prosperous.

Medical Field

▲Dr. Fei Zibin's Honor: The Director of the Japanese Imperial Household Hospital, with more than ten years of chronic illness, was cured by Dr. Fei Zibin of the Menghe School. He then introduced Mrs. Wada Kihachi, the Dean of the East Asia Common Script College, who was suffering from duodenal ulcers, to Dr. Fei for treatment. Her symptoms were physical weakness, severe pain in the left chest and spine three hours after meals, accompanied by vomiting of large amounts of stomach acid. She experienced dizziness and restlessness during the pain, and the pain was more severe in winter. According to the opinions of Japanese surgeons and the diagnosis of Dr. Iwabe, the area was difficult for medication to reach, and the entire duodenum would have to be removed by surgery, with a section of the stomach connected to the esophagus to replace the duodenum. However, Mrs. Wada was afraid of the often-fatal abdominal surgery, so she decided to hire Dr. Fei for treatment. Dr. Fei prescribed two doses of detoxification and suppuration agents and two doses of blood circulation and qi-nourishing agents, and she was completely cured. She has become much healthier and fatter. Therefore, she commissioned the production of a "International Miracle Worker" plaque and asked Professor Kageyama of the hospital to present it to Dr. Fei, and said that traditional Chinese medicine is good at internal medicine, and even surgical diseases can be treated with internal medicine.

▲News of Free Clinic and Medicine Distribution by the Fourth Branch of the Second Special District City Federation: In order to relieve the poor and sick, the Fourth Branch of the Shanghai Second Special District City Federation in the French Concession has established a free clinic and medicine distribution center at the Yixin Temple, Bair Road. They have hired famous doctors, including Dr. Huang Yunong, Fan Zupei, Zhou Yuanpu, Pan Guoxian, and pediatric expert Feng Chengzou, to take turns seeing patients from 8:00 AM to 11:00 AM and from 1:00 PM to 4:00 PM every day from July 1st. In addition to free medical treatment, they also issue medicine certificates, which can be used to obtain medicine from the Shangshoutang Wanxiangchun Pharmacy on Bair Road free of charge. Since the opening of the clinic, more than 700 people have sought medical treatment. The association has also purchased epidemic prevention water, 500 bottles of Jizhong water donated by Shi Dezhi, 360 bottles of Baoan water donated by Lu Wenzhong, 500 bottles of Shanao water donated by Gong Jingyan, and 80 bottles of Baoan water donated by Jicheng Pharmacy, for distribution to citizens. Committee member Dong Wenli, in view of the fact that poor laborers have been seeking medical treatment from the association recently, and some are even unable to pay the registration fee, has issued free registration coupons at the Yuanyuan Business Ground on Pingjili Road, which can be used for free registration at the association, all paid for by Mr. Dong.

No. 18 Reading News 丨Compiled by the Reading Guidance Department of the Shenbao Circulation Library 丨

Table of Contents: 1. Book and Newspaper Introduction 2. Broadcast

Introduction to New Language Forest: This year is the year of humorous essays. Since the publication of The Analects and The Human World, dozens of publications have been advertised as humorous essays. This cannot be said to be a bad phenomenon, but their content either puts on a gentlemanly face or degenerates into low-level interests. There are almost none that can truly take on the task of humorous essays and become popular reading material. As a result, some people fundamentally deny the existence of essays in the current Chinese literary world. Although this is a misunderstanding, to resolve this misunderstanding, essays must be corrected from the aspect of discussing foxes and ghosts.

The New Language Forest, edited by Mr. Xu Maoyong, seems to have this tendency. Opening the first issue, Mr. Du Deji's Alienation, its deep satirical flavor and subtle touch truly make people laugh and cry. Especially in its substance, it exposes reality and educates those backward elements, which is beyond the reach of the so-called humorous essays currently in vogue. In addition, Fengzi's articles are also worth reading. Of course, this publication also has many things like "chats," such as Mr. Chen Zizhan's two prefaces, which are not very suitable for publication here. However, among the current humorous essay publications, it is still the most worthwhile to read. We hope that the editors of New Language Forest will publish more works like Alienation in the future, opening up a small path in humorous essays.

Broadcast: (1) This department notified readers in the 16th issue of this publication who have joined this department but have never communicated that they should explain the reasons for their communication failure to this department in the future. Although 60-70 written explanations have now been received, there are still many readers who have not reported. We hereby solemnly notify that if you still do not explain within this week, your communication qualification will be revoked.

(2) The special reader communication notes specially made by this department have been purchased and used by many readers. Readers have not been able to fill in the forms printed on the notes according to the boxes, and some have even filled in the library card number into the registration number of this department. In the future, we hope that readers will fill in clearly. Also, those who have not registered with this department but communicate with this department are also requested to complete the registration immediately.

(3) Currently, this publication is soliciting short articles from readers on their reading experiences, but very few have been submitted. We hope everyone will work hard to write them.

(4) Due to the hot weather, the office hours of this department have been invisibly shortened. If readers' letters are slightly delayed in replying in the future, please do not be impatient. We are equally absolutely responsible.

(5) Please inform Lin Fei and Cui Dong of your communication addresses.
