Free Talk

In Memory of Mr. Liu Fu

— Chen Zizhan

The Shenbao reported on the 14th, citing a Central News Agency dispatch: "The literary scholar Liu Fu went to the Ping-Sui Railway to investigate dialects a month ago. Due to acclimatization, he returned to Ping with illness. On the 12th, his condition suddenly worsened, and he was readmitted to Xiehe Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. He passed away at 2:10 PM on the 14th. According to the hospital's diagnosis, Liu suffered from jaundice. The root of the disease had been there for a long time, leading to his death. Colleagues in academic circles were deeply saddened upon hearing the news."

Alas! Is Mr. Liu Fu dead! After reading this special dispatch, I couldn't help but feel "sad for a long time"! But I must declare that I didn't "shed tears of sorrow." Because China has lost a linguist, and considering the sake of scholarship, how could we not feel "sad for a long time"! However, I have never met Mr. Liu in person, so hearing the news of his death, I did not dwell on old feelings and "shed tears of sorrow"!

About half a month ago, the Evening News carried a communication from Suiyuan, writing about Mr. Liu's lengthy conversation with this reporter. Mr. Liu talked about his past struggles for the "Literary Revolution" during the May Fourth Movement. He said with some emotion: "Now I have no courage!" We were hoping that Mr. Liu could muster the courage again to continue the struggle and participate in the Mass Language Movement. Unexpectedly, Mr. Liu fell ill and died, and we lost an opportunity to hear the opinions of a linguistic expert. Just speaking about the issue of mass language, this is also a huge loss! Moreover, Mr. Liu's trip to the Ping-Sui Railway was originally to investigate dialects, but he died due to acclimatization. His spirit of dedication to scholarship is truly admirable! Although a regional dialect is not exactly the mass language, if we want to build mass language literature, investigating and studying dialects in various parts of the country, as well as reviewing and answering dialect questions in the mass language, is also an urgent and important task. A scholar like Mr. Liu who was willing to dedicate his life to dialectology could not have his life extended, and he had to abandon his most valuable work. Shouldn't this be something that everyone engaged in the mass language movement should mourn?

A few days ago, I wrote two "Random Talks on New Poetry" and submitted them to the "Trends" section of the Zhonghua Daily. They were triggered by reading Mr. Liu's conversation recorded in the Evening News' Suiyuan communication. I originally planned to talk about Liu's Collection of Earthen Pots written in the Jiangyin dialect in the third section, but I didn't have this book on hand, so I couldn't write it today. Now, based on what I feel, since the emergence of new poetry, there have been more than a hundred published collections of poetry, but only Collection of Earthen Pots can be considered the first collection to be written entirely in dialect. Although it cannot be said to be a great success, compared to those Europeanized poems that people cannot understand (such as the symbolist poems that Mr. Zhao Jingshen considered "incomprehensible" in the preface to the Anthology of Modern Poetry) and the vernacular poems that pile up many classical allusions, Collection of Earthen Pots has its own unique value. Although I don't understand the Jiangyin dialect, I am greatly moved every time I read poems like "The cart rattles through the night, the water is cool, and the wind is blowing" and "Comparing people can be infuriating" in Collection of Earthen Pots. Although he is not like Mr. Liu Dabai, he writes about socialism and labor issues, but the emotional power of his Collection of Earthen Pots is above Mr. Liu Dabai's Collection of Songs of Selling Cloth. It is a pity that he refused to condescend (?) to the position of a farmer poet and did not fully shout out the bitter lives of farmers and the tragic reality of rural areas from his poems with all his life's energy. However, he has already left us with a practical report of writing new poems in dialect, which is also valuable.

I remember when Mr. Liu Fu was in charge of the Women's College, he announced that female students should be called "girls" and not "Miss," which aroused much ridicule and criticism. Fairly speaking, if Mr. Liu only opposed the unnecessary Europeanized elements in the vernacular language, what was wrong with that? Mr. Liu often expressed dissatisfaction with the excessively Europeanized vernacular language. In his General Theory of Chinese Grammar, he said:

I will now give a simple example:

Confucius said: "To learn and practice regularly is not a pleasure?"

This is too old-fashioned, not good!

"To learn and practice regularly," Confucius said, "is not a pleasure?"

This is good!

"To learn and practice regularly is not a pleasure?" Confucius said.

This is even better! Why is it good? It's Europeanized. But "Confucius said" could not be Europeanized to "Said Confucius"!

Mr. Liu's ridicule of the excessively Europeanized vernacular language is still the same as before. The Suiyuan communication in the Evening News carried his conversation with the reporter:

"Promoting the vernacular language is to make it easier for people to understand, but later it became more difficult than classical Chinese, such as excessive Europeanization and meaningless piling up."

He (Mr. Liu) said with great emotion about this point:

"This is something we didn't expect at first!"

That's right, "excessive Europeanization," "meaningless piling up," and "more difficult than classical Chinese" are really the major problems of the currently popular vernacular language (especially vernacular poetry). If the vernacular language had not reached such a dead end, no one would have come out to promote the mass language! Therefore, we can say that if Mr. Liu were still alive, he would one day participate in the mass language movement, or at least he would give a considerable evaluation of this movement from the perspective of a linguist. This assumption is possible. Moreover, Mr. Liu said that he "has no courage now"; in the end, he still has great courage.

Recently, he had a paper, the title of which I forget, about "Namo Amitabha," which was published in the Nanjing Minsheng Daily, and The Analects Monthly also reprinted it. This article of his is probably his most wonderful final work, emitting the last brilliance of his life. This proves that as long as he has life, he is not like many scholars who flatter the powerful like a living corpse who "because the corpse is difficult to decay, temporarily in the air"!

I would like to express my condolences here for Mr. Liu Fu's death. After writing this article, I really couldn't help but feel "sad for a long time"!

Drought

— Xijin

Millions of hearts yearn for rain,

Scorched, a bit of tender seedlings!

Looking up at a round of setting sun,

The evening glow declares the horror of tomorrow.

Occasional clouds are just deception,

Carrying the hope of harvest on the waterwheel.

Sweat from the pores keeps flowing,

The source of life has dried up.

In Memory of Ban Nong

— Shoutong

Yesterday I received the news of Ban Nong's death, which made me recall our meeting a year ago, and I couldn't help but shed tears of sorrow. I remember that last year was also such a summer. Ban Nong's wife returned to Jiangyin first, saying that Ban Nong was studying bells and chimes in Jinan and would return south soon. Sure enough, three days later we met Ban Nong. He even gave me two thin recent works, "Explanation of One" and "Chimes."

One morning we arranged to eat dim sum in Shoushan Park. My younger uncle, Jingbang, was his student, so there was a lot to talk about. Yuan Jiahua was also invited to join us because he was in Jiangyin at his wife's home. We talked about the death of his younger brother, Tianhua, and about his brother's afterlife. Perhaps Ban Nong was too sad, he said many negative things! Finally, Ban Nong also mentioned his childhood experience of not having money to study. He said very emotionally that he would donate his only inheritance—a district map (which can yield 30 shi of rice a year)—to the orphanage as an educational expense for the orphans.

During the meeting, I remember that there was also a student, Mr. Ji, from the Wuxi National Studies Specialized School, who asked Ban Nong many questions about national studies. Ban Nong spoke eloquently, and one could tell that he had been working hard in his studies in recent years.

The thing that Ban Nong talked about most enthusiastically was his professional phonology. Originally, studying Chinese phonology is very boring, but he ran around collecting materials while sweating profusely. As soon as he arrived in his long-separated hometown, he left without warming the seat, busy with work. Four days later, Ban Nong wrote from Qufu, saying that the weather was very hot, but he had obtained a lot of material on bells and chimes. We admired his hard work, but unexpectedly, a year later, his life was sacrificed for his research in the distant Bailing Temple.

We are still extremely grieved by Tianhua's death. Fellow musicians are even more unforgettable. But his brother, Ban Nong, has also died. No matter how the literary world will judge him, I always think Ban Nong is worth crying for.

What I still want to think about now is Ban Nong's wife, who is about forty years old, and two children, as well as Tianhua's family. The district map has been donated. How can they live in a five-room house in the future?

Talking about Malayan Cities (Continued)

— Feier

Johor

Johor, famous in the world for its romantic king.

The Johor Railway Bridge is very famous in Nanyang. The bridge deck is wide, long, and strong, and it has an electrically controlled opening and closing mechanism that allows ships to pass through the open iron gate at a certain stipulated time.

The Johor Royal Palace is built on top of a small mountain. It is surrounded by a bamboo fence with a crescent-shaped flag. It overlooks the Johor Railway Bridge, where cars and horses come and go: cars crawl like strings of tapeworms, and trains squirm on the ground like snakes. The narrow strait between Singapore and Johor is like a piece of white cloth, and the distance of the railway bridge is a blur. At night, a sea breeze makes people's spirits clear from the long days of sleep at the equator, and the moon will turn the earth into a charming scene.

Perhaps it is due to the influence of this charming scenery that the Kingdom of Johor was gently tamed under the British Empire. The King of Johor has now become an empty shell, and the fertile land of Johor has been almost completely presented to the hands of European and American industrialists. As a result, the King of Johor receives a certain salary per year, which is regarded as the price of presenting the territory; and in addition to being directed to sign his name on various notices and orders, he can only roam the world with his English wife. If he doesn't make himself a "romantic king", what else do you want him to do, and what can he do? (The End)

To

— Shao Guanhua

I drifted away with your eyes and died

When the new mud slipped and hurt your tender waist

I wanted to hold you and walk, like the sea

Holds the swallows. I slept immersed in your

Shy kisses, like a small boat

Swinging in the lake, now I suck

Your gaze, and weep silently like

Wrinkles suddenly blowing up in the red clouds,

When you walked away with the shadow of the bamboo branch.

My Translation of "History of the Development of European Literature"丨Reactions to "On Re-translation and Others"丨

— Shen Qiyu

It is rare to buy Shen Bao on the streets of Guangzhou. Today, I happened to get the June 30th issue and saw a lengthy article in the "Free Talk" section by my friend Mu Mutian, which touched upon my translation of "History of the Development of European Literature" and my friend Wang Renshu's "Sociological Art Theory." The publication of both books has some connection to Mu Mutian, so even someone like me, who hasn't written in a year, wants to say a few words.

(Middle omitted) My "History of the Development of European Literature" also has some connection to Mu Mutian. I knew the difficulty of re-translation—especially re-translation from Japanese—so before putting pen to paper, I borrowed the Russian original from Mr. Shiro Omura. However, I don't know Russian, but I knew that Mu Mutian had studied it on his own, so while sweating profusely—it was a hot summer—I searched through the various countries' literary histories in the Oriental Library to find those vast book titles and names that often defied common sense... I should have also taken the Russian text to ask Mu Mutian for guidance. But unfortunately, the word Woruku in the book was neither French nor Japanese, and I didn't have the complete works of Vigny at hand, which made it impossible for me to know that this word meant "wolf," and it also made the person I consulted the other day now discover my "funny mistake," and even come up with the humor that "this wolf traveled to Russia, then traveled to Japan, and then traveled to China, and became Mr. Alke" (?), which I cannot help but feel. Of course, I also know that old friends like Mu Mutian would never make malicious accusations, especially since there are also complimentary words such as "quite faithful" and "this point is naturally the mistake of the Japanese translator." However, a mistake is a mistake after all; when Mu Mutian or others have a more complete translation, my translation will automatically be withdrawn.

According to Mu Mutian's opinion on re-translation,

it is "to act with caution, and it is best to base it on translations in more than two languages." Although I am ignorant, I also know the importance of this point. However, Omura Shiro told me at the time that there were no English, German, French, or other translations of "History of the Development of European Literature," and his translation seemed to be the first of its kind, so I had to take the "expedient" approach as Mu Mutian said (remainder omitted).

I Come From the East (1) Parting Washington in Blossom Season

— Hoshino

Cherry blossoms are in full bloom outside Washington City, and tourists flock to both sides of the Potomac River. Once a year, it is another opportunity for the Japanese to promote "Japanese-American friendship." Because the cherry trees in Washington were a gift from the former Mayor of Tokyo. At that time, Ambassador Saito, who had not been in Washington for long, and his so-called beautiful wife, wore long-sleeved Japanese clothes and led two round, flat-faced children, running back and forth under the cherry blossoms with great pride, showing smiling faces to the tourists. They even published photos taken under the cherry blossoms in American newspapers. During those days, many Japanese goods stores in Washington used cherry blossoms as decorations on their windows. And at every intersection, there were arrow-shaped signs that read: "Cherry Blossom Season is here! Everyone go to the Potomac River to see the cherry blossoms!"

However, this year's cherry blossom season has not been very helpful in promoting the so-called "Japanese-American friendship." Of course, the people of Washington's enthusiasm for cherry blossoms is no less than in previous years, and Ambassador Saito's smile is much more pleasing than that of his predecessor, Ambassador Debuchi! However, Tokyo was then promoting the so-called Asian Monroe Doctrine, wanting the United States to withdraw from the Far East. Americans were tired of Japan playing tricks in the dark; they knew that Saito's smile was forced and hypocritical. An atmosphere of disgust for Japan permeated the United States. And the cherry blossoms of Washington lost a lot of their political function.

The actions of the Japanese in the United States, no matter how small, contain some political function. Their propaganda work is all-pervasive. For example, last year, at the Century of Progress Exposition in Chicago, a Japanese silk tycoon used Japanese silk to make many small pieces of the American flag; distributing them to American tourists. On the one hand, he encouraged them to buy more Japanese silk goods, and on the other hand, he invisibly linked the American's patriotism and goodwill towards Japan. Moreover, when the anti-Japanese sentiment was at its strongest in the United States last year, Japan sent many college students to the United States to show many inexplicable films: inside, they either exposed the corruption and barbarism of the Chinese army, government, and society, or they exaggerated the progress of Japanese construction in Manchuria. They also like to do some small favors to cater to the Americans' preferences. Like sending Japanese stone carvings to various universities; shipping Japanese cherry trees to American cities. The cost is low, and the propaganda value is great. The cherry trees in Washington City have been sent from Japan for many years. This year, a new park was completed in New York, and another large batch of cherry trees was shipped from Tokyo.

Although this year's cherry blossom season in Washington is relatively lacking in political meaning, its artistic meaning is undeniable. On the clear banks of the Potomac River, the willows hang with golden threads. The cherry blossoms are in full bloom like snow, looking a little pink from a distance. Under the trees is a trimmed lawn. When you lean on the railing by the river for a short rest, and look at the Lincoln Memorial made of white stone outside the cherry forest, and the Washington Monument, more than five hundred feet high, reflected in the water. In the slow spring sunshine, it forms a quiet and beautiful picture. You will not believe that just a few feet away is the bustling and noisy center of Washington City.

Page 15

Education News

Resolutions of Various Groups at the Annual Meeting of the Chinese Vocational Education Society The General Assembly Has Concluded

(Nanchang Correspondence) The 14th Annual Meeting of the Chinese Vocational Education Society and the 12th General Assembly of the National Vocational Education Society Discussion, which opened in this province on the 13th of this month, yesterday (the 14th) being the second day of the meeting, at about 6:00 a.m., all 390-odd members arrived at the meeting one after another, and then divided into five groups: Special Group, Education Administration Group, Remedial Education Group, Vocational Curriculum Group, and Rural Improvement Group for group meetings. The morning session was from 7:00 a.m. to 11:00 a.m., then a break was announced. In the afternoon, discussions continued from 3:00 p.m. to 6:00 p.m., and the handling of the cases of each group was completed. Today (the 15th), the general assembly will be held at 9:30 a.m., and the closing ceremony will be held in the afternoon. The results of the group meetings on that day are recorded in detail below,

Special Group Meeting

The Special Committee held a meeting at 6:30 a.m. in the classroom (Humanities Building), chaired by Jiang Hengyuan. The attendees were Huang Yanpei, Zhong Daozan, Tang Ying, Yang Weiyu, Wu Ziqiang, Cheng Shihui, Cheng Shiwei, Zou Shuwen, and Jiang Hengyuan. ㈠ Discussed the method of reviewing the society's proposals. 1. Based on the opinions expressed by the colleagues, when the group meetings are held, observe the nature of the proposals and participate separately. 2. If the discussion results of each proposal require the drafting of a plan by a member, it is hoped that it can be drafted in a timely manner. If this is not possible, it can also be handed over to the Vocational Education Society Office for handling. 3. Identify the central issues. The standards for central issues are as follows: 1. Greater possibility; 2. Emphasis on action; 3. Suitability to needs. 4. Based on the previous standards, two central issues are proposed as follows: 1. Social vocational remedial education; 2. Youth training issues in rural improvement and inter-party liaison issues. The previous issues must be strictly based on the scope of vocational education. 5. The time limit for determining the central issues is tentatively set at three years, and Jiangxi Province will be a special experimental area (especially in the two matters of youth service and remedial education). 6. In order to ensure agile contact between all parties, the Society will set up a communication agency. One, on the reply to President Chiang's telegram, Mr. Wu Ziqiang was recommended to draft it.

Curriculum Group Meeting

At 6:30 a.m. on the morning, the first meeting of the vocational curriculum was held in the Zhinan Room of the Teaching Hall. The attendees were Dai Xizhang, Long Chengzhang, Deng Ruxi, Luo Jingyuan, Zhang Guanghong, Zhang Yuanwei, Jia Foru, Pu Bingjun, Shan Shouwen, Chen Linshi, Liu Gongmu, Ouyang Xuan, Wan Yaozhang, Li Lunhua, Lu Dingfan, Peng Jiemin, Li Yourun, Wu Zhenqiu, Shu Yingchen, Zang Qiji, Liu Jia, Wu Zhiqian, He Qingru, Tie Ming, Yu Yun, Wang Du, Lin Yinshan, Liu Weifu, and others, totaling forty people. The meeting was chaired by Luo Jingyuan. ㈠ The teaching materials for non-vocational subjects in vocational schools should fully develop national consciousness and service skills (proposed by China Vocational School); 2. The citizenship course in vocational schools has no fixed standards, so the society should organize a committee to study it in detail, and request the Ministry of Education to promulgate it as soon as possible (proposed by China Vocational School); 3. Please incorporate national historical sites into the vocational school curriculum (proposed by Zhang Bing) (review opinion) The above three proposals are combined for discussion and renamed "The content of non-vocational subject teaching materials in vocational schools should fully develop national consciousness and service skills." It was resolved in principle to pass it. The method will be formulated in detail by the organization committee of the Society within six months with reference to the contents of the original proposals 1, 2, and 3, and submitted to the Ministry of Education for promulgation as soon as possible. 4. High and junior middle schools across the country should uniformly increase vocational courses and internships that are related to local occupations or customs, in order to cultivate vocational talents who are the backbone of society, and then study specialized academic subjects (proposed by Guo Lingou). Resolution: Retained. 5. The primary school curriculum should be centered on production education, so that the majority of students who cannot go to higher education will have the ability to be independent after graduation and become social producers (proposed by Huang Qingrui). Resolution: Retained. 6. Senior primary schools should add industrial classes (proposed by Zhou Mengyun). 7. Rural primary schools should appropriately add vocational courses to cultivate vocational knowledge among primary school students (proposed by Pan Anye) (review opinion) The proposal was changed to "Rural primary schools may appropriately increase vocational courses as needed according to the environment in order to cultivate vocational knowledge among primary school students." Resolution: The method is in accordance with the original proposal, and an additional clause is added, which will be issued by the Society to the Education Department for implementation. 8. In order to study vocational convenience in practice, please allow students of vocational courses to join internships in agricultural, industrial, and commercial establishments across the country in order to improve vocational skills (proposed by Li Mengxing). Resolution: Passed. The method is revised as follows: 1. Please ask the Ministries of Education and Industry to coordinate with the state-run industrial institutions or factories in various provinces and cities to allow students from various vocational schools to join internships; 2. Please ask the Ministries of Education and Industry to encourage agricultural, industrial, and commercial institutions or factories privately run in various places to accommodate students from various vocational schools to join internships; 3. Students who pass the school or internship results at industrial establishments can graduate. The second meeting was held at 3:00 p.m. The attendees were Lin Yinshan and others, totaling seventeen people. The meeting was chaired by Luo Jingyuan. 9. Revitalizing national thought in order to survive (proposed by Changjingqiao Township Society). Resolution: It will be handled in conjunction with the first proposal. 10. It is proposed to submit to the Ministry of Education to amend the number of class hours for Chinese and English in the senior accounting department (proposed by Zhao Zhuo). Resolution: Request the Ministry of Education to stipulate that the number of class hours for domestic language shall not be less than the number of class hours for foreign language. 11. To promptly determine the standards for vocational education course materials and compile vocational education series of books in order to unify them and promote them widely (proposed by Huang Ji). Resolution: Retained. 12. It is proposed to submit to the Ministry of Education to amend the internship time for accounting vocational schools (proposed by Zhao Zhuo). Resolution: Retained. 13. Should the Ministry of Education's already promulgated curriculum and internship hours for various vocational schools be submitted for revision (temporary motion by Jia Foru)? Resolution: Please ask the Ministry of Education to investigate the actual situation and opinions of vocational schools in various provinces and cities, consider making revisions, and promulgate them separately.

Remedial Group Meeting

At 7:00 a.m., the Remedial Education Conference was held in the library of the teaching hall. The attendees were Shi Yangyong, Tao Moqing, Zheng Wenhan, Yang Chongmu, Wen Zonglu, Liang Zhongyuan, Wu Renqiu, Liang Youci, Lu Aizhi, Tan Da, Shen Tansun, Yang Shili, Liang Bangzhu, Pan Yangyao, Wu Shuzhan, Jiang Songran, and Lu Boyu. The meeting was chaired by Pan Yangyao. ㈠ Discuss the expansion of factories to manage businesses and add remedial classes to popularize schooling for the poor and illiterate. Resolved to amend the proposal to say that vocational schools should make full use of existing internship sites and equipment to run schools. The method will be formulated by the Society and sent to vocational schools across the country for adoption. ㈡ Discuss that the Society's radio station communicates vocational education across the country, and broadcasts vocational education and remedial education, in order to complete the mission of national rejuvenation education. Resolution: The original proposal was passed. Please the Society to handle it with consideration. ㈢ Let remedial education pay attention to women's vocational education. Resolution: Passed, please the Society implement this according to this method. ㈣ Discuss the principle of revitalizing the nation by widely establishing rural remedial schools in rural areas to open up people's wisdom and develop remedial education. Resolution: This proposal is submitted to the Rural Improvement Group for discussion. ㈤ Discuss the compilation and distribution of textbooks for various subjects in vocational remedial schools for use by various schools. Resolution: Passed, please the Society handle it in conjunction with the Vocational Remedial Education Research Association. ㈥ Please order the Education Department to instruct education departments and bureaus in various provinces and cities to order industrial colleges and vocational schools of engineering across the country to set up apprentice classes or technical training classes. Resolved that the proposal be passed, please the Society handle it. ㈦ Agricultural, industrial, and commercial institutions run by the government should allow graduates of vocational schools of the same nature to practice, and give priority to employing trainees with excellent grades to encourage them (representative of Hubei Province Education). ㈧ Vocational school graduates who run small-capital production businesses should request national, provincial, and municipal banks to grant them low-interest long-term loans to encourage them (proposed by the representative of Hubei Education Department). It was resolved that the above two proposals be passed, and the Society is asked to handle them with consideration. ㈨ Wu asked the Ministry of Education to jointly formulate special laws with the Ministry of Industry, and circulate them to industrial and commercial groups across the country, ordering them to raise funds to establish vocational remedial education institutions. All factories and shops should order workers of a certain level to receive vocational remedial education. ㈩ Submit a request to the Ministry of Education to jointly establish vocational guidance and vocational guidance training courses with the Ministry of Interior, and the Ministry of Industry to formulate vocational guidance regulations. ㈠ Youth training in cities and towns should be jointly presided over by vocational schools and vocational remedial schools and industrial and commercial groups. ㈩ ㈡ In addition to remedial vocational skills, the goal of youth training should extremely focus on physical health, training, promoting national spirit, and cultivating service ethics. It was resolved that the above four proposals be passed as they are. ㈩ ㈢ How should vocational mentors be trained in ordinary schools? ㈩ ㈣ Vocational schools should use off-campus equipment to specifically agree with local factories, merchants, and workshops (such as leather shoe making and hairdressing, etc.) as student vocational internship sites based on local and student needs. ㈩ ㈤ The admission qualifications for vocational remedial schools must be subject to considerable literacy education as stipulated by the Ministry, but in fact, some students are recruited who have not received literacy education. If they need to receive remedial education, there is a lack of appropriate textbooks, and primary school textbooks are often used as textbooks, but the time is short and they cannot be taught completely. How should we find a way to remedy this? "Resolution" is merged into the fifth proposal for handling.

Rural Group Meeting

(Morning) At 7:00 a.m., the first Rural Improvement Conference was held in the classroom (Siqi Hall). Seventy-nine people attended. The meeting was chaired by Zhang Luquan. ㈠ Organize an improvement association to expand the scope of rural undertakings (proposed by Du Wenmin). It was resolved that the Society Office should contact relevant agencies to find a way to organize it. ㈡ It is recommended that all provincial departments in the whole car demarcate districts according to the terrain and establish agricultural testing grounds, responsible for improving products, testing soil quality, guiding fertilization, etc., and attaching agricultural training classes to enable the majority of farmers to increase production as much as possible to improve the countryside and revitalize the nation (proposed by Yang Zongkai). "Resolution" retained. ㈢ Submit a request to the National Government to use a part of the temple property across the country to promote rural vocational education (proposed by Xie Baochang). "Resolution" retained. ㈣ The Society should assist the educational administrative authorities of various cities and counties in Jiangsu and Zhejiang provinces to build new rural areas (proposed by Xia Yunong). "Resolution" retained. ㈤ The rural improvement undertakings of each county should be directly guided by the rural normal school to which it belongs, and the graduates of the school should be responsible for handling it, so as to specialize in responsibility (proposed by Wu Yizhong Hong Xiangqu). "Resolution" moved to the administrative group for discussion. ㈥ Rural improvement undertakings should be handled by talents with specialized intelligence and special training (proposed by Miao Gengfang Yingyao). "Resolution" amended and passed. The amendments are as follows: 1. Add "Suggest that all provincial governments of various provinces" before the word "topic," and add "where" before the word "each;" two methods: one, add "by the provincial government order" before the word "each county;" "investigation of each county" changed to "each county investigates;" three, methods 3, 4, and 5 are deleted. ㈦ Select a county in Jiangxi Province that has recovered from banditry as a facility for the entire revitalization of rural production and construction to serve as a county-level autonomous experimental area (proposed by Zhu Yanong). It was resolved in principle to pass it and hand it over to the Society Office for appropriate handling. ㈧ Submit a request to the Central Government to hold a Farmers' Day on a regular basis in accordance with the Children's Day method (proposed by Wang Jieren). It was resolved in principle to pass it, and the date is tentatively set for February 2nd or March 3rd, and it will be handled by the Society Office. ㈨ Ordinary vocational education and rural revitalization (proposed by Tan Bowang). Resolution: Retained. ㈩ Please hold a short-term training class on rural sideline occupations to revitalize the countryside (proposed by Zhang Shui). Resolution: Moved to the administrative group for discussion. ㈩ ㈠ Guiding the cultivation of medicinal herbs to relieve rural bankruptcy (proposed by Wang Hongmei). Resolution: Amended and passed. The amendment is as follows: The original proposal "to relieve rural bankruptcy" is deleted, and the Society should send a letter to the Ministry of Health to formulate methods and order implementation. ㈩ ㈡ Trial run of rural clinics (proposed by Wang Yugang). Resolution: The Society will send a letter to the Ministry of Health to order implementation. ㈩ ㈢ Rural primary schools should implement production education. Resolution: Referred to the "Drafting Committee for Rural Primary School Curriculum Standards" to be organized separately for reference. ㈩ ㈣ It is recommended that the National Economic Commission provide economic and technical assistance to excellent rural improvement institutions across the country. Resolution: In principle, the words "excellent" are deleted, and the words "should have" are changed to "give." ㈩ ㈤ It is recommended that the Chinese Vocational Education Society promptly establish a homespun cloth relief committee. ㈩ ㈥ It is recommended that the Chinese Vocational Education Society promptly organize a silk weaving relief committee. It was resolved that the two proposals be discussed together and referred to the Society Office for reference. ㈩ ㈦ The Ministry of Construction and Education ordered various counties and education bureaus to organize an electro-chemical education committee. Resolution: Amended and passed. The amendment is as follows: The words "organization" and "promotion committee" in the original proposal are deleted. ㈩ ㈧ The Society should send a letter to the Agricultural Science Office of the National Economic Commission and the special commissioner stationed in Nanchang to attend lectures and discussions. Resolution: It was implemented yesterday, and this proposal is not established. ㈩ ㈨ Rural improvement should implement production education. Resolution: Retained. ㈡ ㈩ It is recommended that the central government divide the country into several regions and set up agricultural colleges in each region as a center for promoting local construction. Resolution: Passed. ㈡ ㈠ Revitalizing the nation should be based on improving farmers' livelihoods and improving farmers' knowledge. Resolution: Retained. ㈡ ㈡ Submit a request to the administrative authorities to order all provinces, all townships or several townships belonging to the countryside to organize production and marketing cooperatives to save the rural economic bankruptcy. Resolution: Retained. ㈡ ㈢ Using the market place as the hub for rural improvement. Resolution: Referred to the Society Office for reference. (Afternoon) The second meeting continued at 3:00 p.m., chaired by Zhang Luquan. Matters for discussion: ㈡ ㈣ The complete agriculturalization or local vocationalization of rural primary schools should be drafted separately into a standard draft of the rural primary school curriculum and submitted to the Ministry of Education. Resolution: Please ask the Rural Primary School Curriculum Standards Drafting Committee to be organized separately to handle it. ㈡ ㈤ Promote rural improvement undertakings. Resolution: In principle, it was passed, and Mr. Kang Zhicai, Song Chaiyun, and Sun Younong were recommended to draft an outline and submit it to the General Assembly for discussion. ㈡ ㈥ Please deduct funds from the National Economic Commission's rural improvement funds for Jiangxi to subsidize rural education institutions in Jiangxi to handle agricultural improvement undertakings. Resolution: Amended and passed. The amendment is as follows: In the original proposal method, "rural normal schools and rural primary schools" plus other rural education institutions. ㈡ ㈦ The Ministry of Internal Education and Industry determines the combination of political review and teaching, and implements methods to increase the effectiveness of rural improvement. Resolution: In principle, it was passed. ㈡ ㈧ Submit a request to the National Government to adopt a private-owned state-run land system and establish state-run farms to save the rural crisis. Resolution: In principle, it was passed and referred to the Society Office for appropriate handling. ㈡ ㈨ Please ask the Ministry of Education to stipulate that at least one school supervisor in each county must have studied rural education in order to urge and guide the rural improvement projects in each county. Resolution: Passed. ㈢ ㈩ Revitalizing the nation should widely establish rural areas in rural areas, establish rural remedial schools, open up people's wisdom, and develop remedial education as a principle. Resolution: Retained. As for the results of the Education Administration Group meeting, because the discussion time was too late and it was not organized in time, it is omitted.

Middle School Graduates in This City Held a Joint Graduation Ceremony Yesterday ▲ The ceremony was solemn in the City Hall Auditorium ▲ About 2,000 guests and graduates attended ▲ Mayor Wu and Director Pan and others delivered speeches

The third joint graduation ceremony of secondary schools in the city was held in the auditorium of the city government at 9:30 a.m. yesterday. The ceremony was quite grand. The details are recorded as follows:

Number of Participants

The participants yesterday included Mayor Wu Tiecheng, Director of the Education Bureau Pan Gongzhan, Director of the Social Affairs Bureau Wu Xingya, Standing Committee Member of the Municipal Party Committee Tao Baichuan, and guests Liu Zhanen, Liao Maoru, Zhu Yingpeng, Chen Renhe, principals and teachers of various middle schools, graduates, etc., totaling about 2,000 people.

Situation at the Venue

The graduates of each school went to the city government to assemble before 9:30 a.m., led by the principals or teachers of each school. Chen Section Chief, Jiang Section Chief, Inspector Ma, and Commissioner Zhou of the Municipal Education Bureau personally received the guests and the students rested in the large cafeteria. At 9:30 a.m., they were arranged in the auditorium, divided into senior high, junior high, A, B, C grades, etc. in a very good order. The Municipal Public Security Bureau military band and the Municipal Health Bureau ambulance team were all present to provide services.

Order of Ceremony

1. Opening and playing music; 2. Singing the Party song; 3. Paying three bows to the national flag, school flag, and Sun Yat-sen's portrait; 4. Respectfully reading Sun Yat-sen's will, silent mourning; 5. Chairman's report; 6. Awarding graduation certificates, playing music; 7. Awarding prizes; 8. Mayor's speech; 9. Speech by the representative of the Municipal Party Committee; 10. Guest speeches; 11. Graduate representative's reply; 12. Photography; 13. Ceremony completed, playing music.

▲ Tongyi Junior High School, total of five students

Chairman's Report

Chairman Pan Kung-chan, Master of Ceremonies Peng Chu-chi, Recorders Chou Hsien-chu and Chou Chao-nan. The ceremony was performed as scheduled. First, Chairman reported the results of the joint entrance examination, briefly stating that there were 1,403 students from 51 senior high schools and 2,147 students from 72 junior high schools participating in this year's examination, totaling 3,550 people. The results showed that 951 students from senior high schools passed, accounting for 67%, and 1,612 students from junior high schools passed, accounting for 75%, for a total of 2,563 students passing. According to regulations, all should participate in the graduation ceremony. However, due to the fact that some have already left Shanghai and some have taken college entrance examinations, they cannot attend today. The above refers to general academic subjects. In addition, the number of vocational subject graduates who did not participate in the examination is not yet certain because the schools have not yet reported to the Education Bureau, but it is roughly estimated to be around 1,000 people. It is estimated that there are more than 3,500 graduates this year. The Education Bureau has submitted a request to the municipal government and the Ministry of Education to include award standards in the examination regulations. Students who score A in each subject and rank in the top three in overall average will be awarded scholarships and certificates. Students who score B or higher in each subject and rank in the A grade in overall average will be awarded certificates. Schools with A grade performance will also be awarded certificates.

Mayor's Admonitory Speech

Following this, the Mayor presented certificates and delivered an admonitory speech, briefly stating that the reason why the joint graduation ceremony for middle schools is held at the Municipal Government is because we consider the joint graduation ceremony for middle schools to be a very important event. You all know that there are 450 million people in China, and very few have the opportunity to study. Even fewer have the opportunity to receive higher education. Therefore, we believe that your graduation from middle school is hard-earned and deserves a grand ceremony. From now on, the joint graduation ceremony for all schools in Shanghai will be held at the Municipal Government every year. After graduation, some of you will pursue further studies and some will seek employment. But whether you pursue further studies or seek employment, never forget the kindness of the nation, society, parents, and elders towards you. Always strive to repay them. Those who will pursue further studies must study diligently and not give up halfway. After acquiring advanced knowledge, dedicate what you have learned to the nation and society, so that the nation and society will have one more citizen with advanced knowledge and gain more benefits. Those who will seek employment in the future must also be very loyal to the nation and society and contribute your knowledge and abilities. This is how you will not fail the cultivation of the nation, society, parents, and elders, and this is how you will repay their kindness. Today, China is in extreme danger, and the people of the whole country are in a state of instability. It is just like a dilapidated house and a broken boat, swaying in the wind and rain, amidst the surging waves. If we want to save it, we must have the people of the whole country united and of one mind. Especially those who are educated should bear more responsibility. You must understand that today is not a time to enjoy comfort, but a time to endure hardship and bide our time. It is a time to make meals, not a time to eat meals. It is a time to build houses, not a time to live in houses. At present, everyone wants to eat ready-made meals and live in ready-made houses, which has led to everyone having no food to eat and no houses to live in. Therefore, we must create a new world. Those who study agriculture should go to the countryside, those who study engineering should do engineering, and those who study mining should do mining. Do not all go down the same path. Whether you seek employment or pursue further studies, if you can recognize this point clearly, the future of the country will be bright. Only then will you not fail the cultivation of the nation, society, parents, and elders, and only then will you have repaid their kindness.

Party Department Address

Tao Pai-chuan, the representative of the Municipal Party Department, stated briefly that the Mayor just said that whether you pursue further studies or seek employment, you must repay the nation and society. But among you, there must be many who cannot pursue further studies and have no jobs to take. How should we strive to repay them? Ordinary people think that not being able to pursue further studies means dropping out of school. This is wrong. Pursuing further studies certainly provides an opportunity to study, but not being able to pursue further studies also allows you to study. After graduating from junior high school, you have a small foundation in various subjects and can study on your own. Rather than going to a depressed school, it is better to study on your own at home. Many famous people in society have never attended college but have become famous. Secondly, there is unemployment. At your age, there is no talk of unemployment. Your age is not the time for employment, but the time for study. That is, you must not drop out of school. Studying on your own at home is not unemployment. Moreover, careers must be created by oneself. In the countryside, you can educate children under thatched roofs. In the city, you can set up public schools near factories. As long as you actually do it, you don't have to worry about society not helping. Finally, we must understand that the fundamental reason why China has come to this point is the aggression of imperialism. We must work hard to abolish unequal treaties and drive out the forces of imperialism. Only then can we pursue further studies and seek employment.

Guest Speakers

Next, guest speakers addressed the audience. Wu Hsing-ya, the director of the Social Affairs Bureau, stated briefly that China is now in a semi-colonial position. Since the September 18th Incident, the national crisis has become even more serious. The Chinese problem has led to the inability to maintain world peace and the inevitability of world war. When this world war breaks out, the elderly and middle-aged will of course stand at the forefront and sacrifice themselves to seek survival for the country and the nation. But those who continue the elderly and middle-aged to seek survival for the country and the nation are actually the young students. You must constantly work hard. In the world war, you are the new life of the Chinese nation. The responsibility of revitalizing the nation and building the country rests on you. I pray that you will work hard. Liao Mao-ju, Liu Chan-en, Chen Jen-ho, and others also spoke. The speeches were lengthy and will be omitted.

Student Reply

Finally, Director Pan gave an admonitory speech, encouraging students to strengthen their physique and pay attention to discipline. Then, representatives of the graduates, Chen Ho-kun from Chingyeh Senior High School and Hu Hsi-ping from Nanyang Model Junior High School, gave their replies. Afterwards, a group photo was taken and the ceremony concluded.

New Tennis Techniques (7)

Originally written by J. PARMLY PARET

Translated by Chien Yi-chin and Hong Chun

丨Copyright Reserved. Reproduction Prohibited

Chapter 3 Starting the Match丨Serving

▲ Research on Serving Posture, Technique, and Direction of Force

Serving is the beginning of each game in a match. Players should use a draw to determine who has the right to serve first (it is generally considered that serving first is beneficial). This privilege is granted to the opponent only after the end of one game, and is enjoyed alternately in each game until the end of the match.

When serving, players are subject to extreme restrictions. At this time, they should stand in the designated position, with both feet not crossing the baseline or touching the baseline. The serving position should be in the middle of the baseline and the sideline, alternating between right and left. The ball served should pass over the net and land within the opponent's diagonal service area before the receiver returns the ball.

The biggest restriction for the server is that the ball served can only land in a very narrow position in the opponent's court. Unlike ordinary shots, the opponent's court is completely open. When serving, the ball can only land within the opponent's diagonal service area. This service area only accounts for about one-quarter of the entire court. However, due to the obstruction of the net, a large part of the service area near the net is completely useless. The area where the ball can land is only the 5 or 6 feet of the court behind. Therefore, in reality, it only accounts for one-tenth of the entire court.

When serving, it is important to hit the ball very hard so that it flies out quickly and passes over the net, landing in the designated service area in the opponent's court. At this time, an attacking method must be used to quickly land the ball in a position that is difficult for the receiver to deal with. The server's agile attack and the receiver's agile response are both important parts of tennis technique.

The server has two chances to serve. Therefore, taking advantage of this point, many people who can hit the ball take the opportunity to make the first ball served fierce and difficult to receive. But if the first serve is unfortunately missed, it is even more important to concentrate and be careful, and not to repeat the same mistake the second time, thus losing a point. Because continuing to miss the serve twice counts as losing one point. The actual serving method used today is to throw the ball upwards, raise the arm high, pass over the head, and hit. If this is the case, both feet should be parallel to the trajectory of the ball, and the body should be sideways to the net, as if hitting in the court. Therefore, the left foot (for a player serving with the right hand) should be placed just behind the baseline. When hitting the ball, it is like a woodcutter holding an axe to chop a tree, but another hand cannot be used to help.

Since there are two chances to serve, the server should hold two balls in his left hand, or even three at the same time (but the author does not approve of holding three). When preparing to serve, one ball is held in the palm of the left hand, and the other ball is clamped between the thumb and forefinger. At this time, the technique is to throw the ball exactly into the predetermined hitting space. Therefore, long-term training is required to be able to do this as desired each time. When the ball has already been thrown into the air, it is too late to move the body to hit it, and moving will definitely affect the hitting and cause a miss.

When beginners serve, it is a very big mistake to hold only one ball in the left hand, but they prefer to do so, and do not pay attention to the consequences of this bad habit. You must know that the first mistake in serving is unexplainable, so the second one should be sent out immediately, simply and without looking around to change the position. It is already extremely difficult for the server to accurately determine the place where the ball will land and estimate the angle, speed, and trajectory of the ball. Therefore, after the calculation has been done, if there is a mistake the first time, the second time it is necessary to discover the original orientation. If only one ball is held in the left hand, then after the first mistake, it is necessary to move the position to pick up another ball. As a result, the angle in the eye will naturally change when serving for the second time, and the result of the second time may be worse than the first.

A Record of Lingering Fragrance

— Originally written by Princess Der Ling of the Qing Dynasty Translated by Qin Shou-ou

I never expected him to joke with me, and I didn't even notice if he had knelt down himself. I believed it was true and fell down with a thud. Later, everyone laughed, and I realized that I had been tricked. Perhaps the Empress Dowager hadn't even gotten up yet! Poor Guangxu, in name he was an emperor, but how lonely and sad he was! He could only find some happiness from such childish and insignificant jokes, which was so tragic! At that time, I was deceived by him, and I laughed with him once, but after thinking about it, I couldn't help but cry for him! I can say categorically that apart from this kind of boring joke, he couldn't find any more happiness. He couldn't do the things he loved to do in his heart, but he had to do the things he didn't love to do. In short, no matter where he went, he was always a prisoner!

Our train had to stop at night. Probably the movement of the train at night would inevitably disturb the Empress Dowager's peace. Once the train stopped, all sounds also disappeared. In this way, could the Empress Dowager rest peacefully? No, no. With the Empress Dowager's dignity, how could she be exposed in the wilderness without any defense! Therefore, every time our train stopped, a train of soldiers following closely behind would also stop. Hundreds of fully armed guards were busy climbing out of the darkness and quietly setting up sentries around our train. And the (Guangxu's car also had huge blue dragons painted on both sides.) two cars next to the Empress Dowager and Guangxu were guarded especially closely, simply completely surrounded. However, the Empress Dowager herself could still get off the train freely, as long as she was happy. But Guangxu could not cross the line, and no one else was allowed to go up. It can be said that he was completely isolated from all people and things in the world, no different from a lonely ghost in solitude. Only in his dreams could he temporarily jump out of this big circle where evil demons were hiding everywhere. (84)

Mulberry Picking Girl

— Ren Wei

Every season when the first silkworms spin their silk, I think of the mulberry picking girls with cloths wrapped around their foreheads. They are all diligent and frugal women who can endure hardship. They get up early in the morning and sleep late at night, and they can't sleep well at night either. At least they have to feed the silkworms with mulberry leaves three or four times.

In the morning, before the sun comes out of the mountains, they wrap those cloths around their foreheads, taking advantage of the dew on the mulberry leaves that hasn't been dried by the sun, and go to pick mulberries one by one without even combing their hair. Those who travel long distances carry a dry food bag to fill their hunger along the way. Among these mulberry picking girls, it can be said that there are simple, pretty, old, and young ones, but they are mostly healthy young women. They don't need men to help them pick. Their physique is much stronger than that of men in our cities! And that kind of diligent and healthy virtue really makes the fashionable girls in the city who wear long cheongsams and put on yellow rouge feel ashamed!

Sometimes, their gentle demeanor can easily touch the hearts of every young and passionate man. They often use a moving tone to sing a southern country love song. Sometimes, when they hear their tones, they can't help but sing back to each other. But they will never shamelessly allow a man to find a secluded mountain depression and indulge in licentiousness like those southern barbarians. But the anecdotes of "Sangjian Pushang" may not be absent.

But in recent years, under the pressure of the rural economic bankruptcy, the poor rural women are in a hurry to think about how to fill their empty stomachs first. They seem to have little leisure to think about flirting.

The Eighteen Scenic Spots of Xuanmiao Temple in Suzhou

— Nan Gong Sheng

People who visit West Lake in Hangzhou all know that West Lake has eighteen scenic spots. Few know that Xuanmiao Temple in Suzhou also has a legend of eighteen scenic spots. However, the eighteen scenic spots of West Lake are natural landscapes, so they still exist today and can be pointed out. The eighteen scenic spots of Xuanmiao Temple in Suzhou, however, are partly man-made and partly lost, and there is no definite research, so they have been lost and are not taken seriously. According to the legend, the eighteen scenic spots of Xuanmiao Temple in Suzhou are: the Wordless Tablet, the Large Water Vat, the Hexagonal Pavilion Pillar Bases, the Five Hundred Arhats, the Stone Railing with Nails, the Miro Pavilion, the Terrace, the Three Pure Ones Bodhisattva, the Stone Pillar, the Soaring Furnace, the Bronze Man, Mount Wudang, the "Wonderful Unity of Origin" Plaque, the Twin Wells, the Heng and Ha Generals, the White Bark Poplar, Niu Jiao Bang Urine Buckets, and the Old Woman Buying Thread at the Main Entrance. However, most of them can no longer be seen today.

The Wordless Tablet, the Large Water Vat, the Terrace, the Three Pure Ones Bodhisattva, the "Wonderful Unity of Origin" Plaque, and the Heng and Ha Generals are six scenic spots that anyone who goes to Xuanmiao Temple can see. The Miro Pavilion has been burned down, and the Zhongshan Hall has now been rebuilt. The stone pillars are the stone pillars of the Miro Pavilion, and they are all elaborately crafted with two arms' span, so naturally they were also destroyed in the fire. The Twin Wells are on the side of the abbot's room. Mount Wudang is an antique in the Ancestor Hall. There was a fact that Taoists wanted to steal and sell it before. The Bronze Man is also an antique in the Ancestor Hall. The Stone Railing with Nails is a stone railing on the terrace, covered with iron nails. The Hexagonal Pavilion Pillar Bases are on the side of the Sanfang Chang Tea House. These seven scenic spots can be found with careful investigation. The Soaring Furnace was a large incense burner in front of the Miro Pavilion, but it is no longer there. The White Bark Poplar was burned to death along with the Miro Pavilion during the fire. The Five Hundred Arhats were built on the roof ridges of the main entrance of Xuanmiao Temple and the Three Pure Ones Hall, but now they are also fragmented and cannot be seen again. As for the two scenic spots, Niu Jiao Bang Urine Buckets and the Old Woman Buying Thread at the Main Entrance, let alone now, they cannot be seen. Even twenty years ago, they were already gone. It's just that in the past, dozens of urine buckets were lined up in the Niu Jiao Bang area, and from the main entrance to below the terrace, they were full of old women selling thread, so they became two scenic spots. How can they be seen again today?

General Mobilization

Rowing the Incense Boat

— Xu Xiaoting

The inland cities and villages are indeed too lifeless. Here, there are many temple fairs and incense festivals to embellish them. Therefore, a layer of liveliness floats on the dull streets. Prohibiting superstition and overthrowing theocracy are out of the question in rural society.

During each incense festival, the owner of the incense boat holds the most special power. They support a bare-backed boat, rocking from east village to west village, gathering many Taoist priests and nuns, and heading to their destination in the sound of oars.

Although the life of rowing the incense boat can earn a few copper coins from the yellow cloth pocket of every old woman, the most annoying thing is waiting for the Taoist nuns to board the boat, taking incense, taking food, greeting you, I look at you, first gather on the shore, and then a wooden fish, a cry of Amitabha, slowly like a car slowly running on the boat. In the splashing of water and the sound of oars, the Taoist nuns sit on both sides of the boat's gunwale, very devoutly knocking on wooden fish, chanting Buddhist scriptures, and adjusting the silent air to move forward. After each Buddhist chant, there can be a lot of conversations. What they say is either that Wang's sister-in-law in the village is stealing a man, or how badly Li's old woman treats her daughter-in-law. The owner of the boat only knows to row forward, and everything else is not in his heart.

The inland incense period is today in Dongzhen and tomorrow in Xicun, so the Taoist nuns can burn incense one after another. The owner of the incense boat also works in order. They not only get the fare from the Taoist nuns, but also get special wine money from the temple host. Their life is comfortable and open. This way of making a living is indeed a special occupation in the countryside.

Northeast Fourth Company Commander

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Thirty-Two: The General Indulges in Pleasure All Day Long; Few Soldiers Return Amidst the Cries of Old and Young.

Gui Zhi saw that this matter seemed not unrelated. Taking advantage of the time to collect the Lantern Festival items and go to the wall lattice, she took out the tea jar, poured fragrant tea leaves into it with boiling water from the kettle on the stove in the room, and then, after rolling the tobacco leaves, and lighting the lamp, gave them all to Zhao Weng, and poured a cup of hot tea, placing it on the corner of the table next to Zhao Weng. Only then did she retreat to the chair opposite and sit down. Zhao Weng drank a cup of tea, first speaking to the Jiang family, who was sitting next to him, "Old Madam, it's not that I'm praising you, but your daughter is really well-educated. These days, people's hearts are too malicious; just a simple comparison brings out the good people." Hearing these words, Jiang was confused, not knowing where they came from. She smiled and said, "You're still saying that; the child is a member of your family, whether she's good or bad is your family's business. Old Master, you love your son, and in turn, you love your daughter-in-law." Zhao Weng said, "There's a reason I'm saying this; why would I just blindly praise my own children? Speaking of this, he sighed again and said, "People's hearts are really hard to tell. That Miss Huang Manying and Company Commander Tian were very close; according to what people saw, there was no problem with them marrying, right? Look, I'm also seeing a big change in people's hearts. I'm even using a new term." Hearing these words, Gui Zhi understood a bit in her heart. Actually, it wasn't anything surprising; she had known for a long time that Huang Manying had a cousin. But she couldn't reveal this first, so she straightened her face and said, "What's wrong with her?" Zhao Weng said, "It's something no one would have expected; she's become friends with Gan Erye." Hearing these words, Gui Zhi really didn't believe it, but she still held her breath and listened. Zhao Weng said, "If I hadn't seen it with my own eyes, I wouldn't have believed it. Just last night, I saw Gan Erye walking down the street arm-in-arm with her." Jiang quickly glanced at Gui Zhi, and then replied to Zhao Weng, "How would they know each other?" Zhao Weng said, "That's what I'm saying. When I met the two of them last night, it was Miss Huang who greeted me first, so I naturally stood there and talked." (435)

World News

A Tour of Europe

— Zhang Ruogu

▲ Letter from Berlin (Part 1)

While in retreat at the Maranouchi Monastery in Belgium, I received a letter from Berlin, Germany. The sender was Mrs. E. Schnider, who lives in Leuven. Her husband is the secretary of the Belgian envoy to Germany. Knowing that I am an admirer of metropolises, she especially described the scenery of Berlin in her letter. I have long yearned for the major cities of Eastern Europe, and if I have the opportunity in the future, I would very much like to go to Berlin, Vienna, Budapest, and other places on an art tour. Below is a depiction of Berlin translated from Mrs. Schnider's letter.

Berlin is one of the most modern cities in the world, a bustling metropolis. From morning to night, the sounds of the city are noisy everywhere, and the wheels and whistles of cars are constantly rolling and whistling there.

Such a capital is the center of the outstanding people of a strong country, and the hub that demonstrates the strong Germanic spirit.

Near the central station, the scenes that have already begun to move early in the morning, and the bright red and green advertising posters, are dazzling. The number of residents in a single city is almost equal to the entire population of Belgium, which will of course arouse endless interest from a curious Belgian tourist.

We are now under the bronze statue of William I, surrounded by other bronze statues stained with green. Not far from here, you can see the vast Schloss villa, with its Greek temple-style facade and jungle-like stone pillars.

When crossing the streets, it is best to always walk on the yellow sidewalk, because the traffic on the road is constant. If you are not careful, you may lose your life. We should admire the precision of the road administration facilities. Although the traffic on the road is very congested, there are no police officers to be seen. Various vehicles obey the command of the special lights, and the order is orderly and without confusion. What a solemn and beneficial discipline!

Everywhere, there are interlaced vehicles, elevated trams, buses, freight cars, cars, and bicycles: browsing these disciplined people almost makes people forget the time to eat. The various restaurants make it difficult to choose to follow, and the ingenious food on the menu makes people sigh. If you have the opportunity to come to Berlin to eat, I recommend a good thing. Do not forget to taste the taste of Delicaiesses de la Baltigue!

You want to know how much it costs? When you settle the bill, you will definitely lengthen your face:::

After dinner, go to a dessert shop for tea. This dessert shop has seven large living rooms and seven orchestras. In the not vaserland restaurant, the layout is very beautiful. In a corner of the hall, we can overlook the artificial natural scenery, a panoramic view of the Alps, the banks of the Rhine River, and the sudden sunrise, and the sudden wind and rain. We can see real rain and lightning:::

Business News

September Contract for Gold Bar Opens High, Falls Instead; Increase in Bullish Chips in August; Total of 17,528 Taels

Difference Between Near-Term and Forward Cotton Yarn Gradually Widening

▲ Bulls Tend Toward Forward Contracts: No Intention to Take Delivery This Month

The yarn market is slightly weak due to a slight drop in American cotton. Bullish investors are taking profits, causing the market to loosen. Moreover, those taking delivery this month are still lacking. Although sentiment is good, there are not many buyers for near-term contracts, and interest is solely focused on forward contracts. Therefore, the price gap between near-term and forward contracts is widening. Given this situation, arbitrage will still be the only way to make profits in the future. The yarn market’s current situation makes it difficult to be optimistic.

Cotton Fields Decrease, US Cotton Rises by 100 Points Last Week

New York, July 13th, telegraphed the cotton market situation last week, saying that an unexpectedly favorable cotton field report for the bulls caused cotton prices to rise by about one point per pound. However, the cotton market eventually retreated slightly due to profit-taking and selling in the South. Although speculative demand is still active, purchases by the trade are relatively flat. The actual position of the cotton market can now be considered slightly weak, as accumulation has been quite heavy recently. Spot demand in the South has also not improved significantly. The cotton field report has provided the trade with a solid basis for calculating possible production. The most important factor in the future is the weather. Temperatures in Texas remain abnormally high, and the north and west urgently need rain. It is heard that in drier areas, cotton crops have deteriorated. However, in areas with favorable weather, cotton crops have made progress. Cotton crop conditions elsewhere are mostly either good or fair. Although there have been showers in the Gulf states of the eastern United States, there have been no reports of significant increases in boll weevil. The cotton market is slightly firmer than before, and cloth factories are now raising prices.

Indian Cotton Market Prices Rise Last Week

Last week, the cotton market rose because the government cotton field report in the US showed reduced cotton fields. Before the new cotton moves, the market situation will favor buyers. Export inquiries vary, with Europe being quiet and Japan being more active than before, especially for Central Indian Gandhi and Lijas cotton. The weather is very good, and various places have started ginning preparations. The appended statistics for last week are as follows (in thousands of bales):

Grain and Flour Continue to Rise

▲ Transaction Volume Greatly Increased: Forming a Short Squeeze

Yesterday, after the opening of the flour market in the morning, prices for all months showed a huge rise again, and the prosperity of transactions was unprecedented in recent years. The volume in half a day reached a huge 1.89 million bags. The chaos and disorder in the market were also the first in several years. When opening prices were set, due to domestic and foreign situations, either continuous rain caused disasters, or droughts exerted their power. Therefore, the excitement of the people was an inevitable fact. In addition, grain prices in the north were expensive due to water and drought imbalances. It was said that the spot price in Tianjin had increased to six cents, opening at 2.23 to 2.28 yuan. Therefore, the opening price for this month was 26 cents, and then gradually increased, forming a short squeeze. Factories are preparing themselves, and outside short sellers are also rushing to cover, so the highest squeeze was to 29.5 cents. The rise in prices for forward months was certainly also crazy, but many bullish investors were taking profits at high prices, and factories were also selling. Although transactions were also very prosperous, the increase was only ten to twenty cents. This situation was caused by natural disasters. If Heaven favors us and sweet rain comes, then the huge terror may be slightly suppressed. Otherwise, the potential is very large, and there is little opportunity for loosening. As a result, it rose 5.5 cents compared to the previous week, 2.75 cents in August, 2.5 cents in September, 1.75 cents in October, 2.5 cents in November, and 2 cents in December.
