100,000 Bags of Foreign Rice Newly Contracted ▲ 4.15 Yuan Per 100 Jin ▲ Foreign Rice Market Fluctuates

Yesterday, the situation of foreign rice first saw people feeling very panicked because the drought in the south had already occurred, and the north had suffered a flood again. The inland and hoarding households on this street became even more eager to buy, and the market price of Jijing rice rose to 9.4 yuan. The prices of all other types of rice also increased. Then, because the soybean and rice industry had already restricted rice prices and made a resolution to order foreign rice, and even planned to request the elimination of foreign rice taxes, the sentiment in the market turned downward. It was heard that various rice shops had urgently contracted with foreign merchants to immediately load 100,000 bags of No. 1 Saigon rice (some say the first batch was 5,000 tons, and the second batch has not yet been decided). The contracted price was 4.15 yuan per 100 jin in national currency, with tariffs and water transport fees added separately. In total, calculated at 150 jin per sack, the combined price should be below 10 yuan. This price is already close to the current market price. If rice prices rise further in the future, or if taxes can be reduced or exempted, then the contracting parties can profit. After hearing this news, the appetite of buyers in the market weakened. The Xiaojiao rice, which had been rising for days, immediately fell from 8.8 yuan to 8.5 yuan. Once sentiment stabilized, the market price also decreased slightly. A total of 12,000 bags of rice were offered on the market, mostly bought by shops on this street, with northern and inland regions buying a little over 1,000 bags each.

Rice Prices Continue to Fall After Price Controls

(South Shanghai) Yesterday, each guild had only 17 or 18 source vessels (a total of 2,600-2,700 stones of goods). Since the price controls were imposed once, market sentiment has turned flat. Only the Weihaiwei guild bought 600-700 bags. The market for special late rice continued to show a downward trend. The prices of Changbang Sutong Nangang and other japonica rice and Qingjiao Songsi Xilian and other late rice fell again by ten to twenty cents. Only Du Yangjian and Bianyuan and other types of rice with scarce supply still saw a stable situation.

(North Shanghai) Yesterday, the source of goods from the various rivers was 12 or 13 vessels. The appetite for various goods in the market was normal. Early japonica rice was slightly traded. Baiyuan and various pointed rice were sold in small quantities. Except for a small drop in the price of white japonica rice, the prices of other goods did not fluctuate much.

Jiujiang New Soybeans Suddenly Rise by Twenty Cents

Yesterday, the price of yellow soybeans was unchanged from the end of last week, but the demand was not weak, and sentiment stabilized. It is estimated that factories bought about fifteen or sixteen carts of Yingzhou beans and Bengbu beans. Small retailers on this street bought two carts of Zhengyangguan beans. The second batch of Jiujiang Xinchengmen soybeans arrived at the port yesterday. The quantity was small, and the quality was also inferior. A total of 214 bags arrived, causing distorted sentiment among buyers. They argued over prices, so the market suddenly rose by twenty cents to 3.40 yuan. The Ningbo guild bought them. According to people in the industry, the quality of soybeans yesterday was not good, and the market situation did not rise sharply.

North-South Goods: Lanzhuzhi and Lanhua Seeds Debut

The Lanzhuzhi and Wuyezhi produced in Zhangzhou this year are expected to be bountiful, and the costs are higher. It is difficult to set a price. It is said that the products this year are better than last year, so the Taikoo steamship imported a small amount for trial marketing yesterday. The total was less than 30 boxes. The cost of Lanzhuzhi is 40 yuan, and the cost of Wuyezhi is 26 to 27 yuan. If the quality is excellent, it may be possible to maintain a profit.

The number of new Lanhua seeds this year is not high. The first batch of over ten boxes arrived yesterday. The quality is still yellow and bright, but half of them are of lower quality. As the number is small, they should sell well.

Sugar Market: Less Local Refined White Sugar Shipped

Yesterday, the trend in the sugar market remained flat. The guild allocated a disk of 24 raw sugar white spot goods at the original price, but it was unsuccessful. The price of goods in this warehouse was 20 yuan, down 5 cents from the previous day. The price of transit goods was 6.4 yuan, and the price of Dutch red transit goods was 6.3 yuan. The price of Taikoo B mark was 20.4 yuan. Recently, due to the hot weather, most of the workers in this factory have stopped working, so there is a shortage of refined white sugar shipped. The original price of 19 yuan has not been widely offered. Yesterday, 400 bags of Hainan red sugar were opened, with high-grade sugar at 13 yuan and secondary sugar at 12.7 to 12.8 yuan. Dozens of bags of high-grade refined red sugar were opened at 16 yuan.

Silk and Tea: New Silk Sales Frequent and Smooth

▲ New White Filature Silk Transported to Hangzhou: Silk weaving merchants in Hangzhou purchased a significant amount of new white filature silk in Shanghai after the new cocoons came on the market. Various manufacturers reeled and unravelled them one after another and transported them to Hangzhou in batches. In the first half of this month, a total of 135 bales of new cocoon white filature silk were transported to Chang'an Changshanmen stations to meet the needs of the machines, all of which were B grade 20-22 denier.

▲ New Re-reeled Silk Transported to Shanghai, Zhejiang, and Huzhou: This year's spring cocoons were abundant. Because the price of fresh cocoons was low, many silkworms spun their own native silk. The native silk collected by silk shops in Xun (Nanxun) and Zhen (Zhenze) was re-reeled by various weaving households to make large re-reeled dry silk and transported to Shanghai to sell to foreign firms. Because there has been no rain for a long time since the beginning of summer and the inland river water is shallow, transportation by wheel is difficult. Therefore, the re-reeled silk stored in various producing areas is now being rushed to Shanghai in batches. In the past half month, 220 pieces of all grades of white dry silk have been loaded by small Shenhu ferries and stored in silk warehouses for sale.

▲ New York's Imports of Japanese Silk Remain Strong: Silk weaving factories in New York are on vacation due to the extreme heat, and the silk market is unusually quiet. Imports of Japanese silk remain strong. The current silk price has plummeted again. The standard Japanese silk is only offered at slightly over US$1.10 per pound, which is another drop of 400 yuan per bale in Chinese currency.

▲ Zhejiang's Summer Cocoons Have a Poor Harvest and Inferior Quality: Zhejiang's summer cocoon harvest this year is poor, and the cocoons are not thick. Few Shanghai silk merchants went to Zhejiang to buy summer cocoons. Yesterday, 74 jin of new model cocoons were transported from Haining to Shanghai and have now been sent to the factory for trial reeling. It is said that the baking yield is over 400 jin.

▲ American Firms Hoard Filature Silk: European and American firms in this port, seeing that New York's silk inventory is only enough for a little over a month of demand, and that the cloth factories will inevitably replenish raw materials after the summer vacation starts, and that the price of white filature silk has fallen to the lowest limit, are taking the opportunity to depress prices and buy. Those manufacturers with more cocoons in hand have to sell at a loss to maintain operations. It is estimated that Jardine and others bought 130 bales of Grade B new white filature silk, but the price is still not strong.

Luzhuang Zhenmei Tea Continues to Fall

Yesterday, the foreign tea market in this port saw brisk sales of Zhenmei silk tea from Luzhuang, but since the price of Wuyuan Zhenmei fell last week, British and French firms have been consistently stringent in their assessment of goods from Tunxi, Shexian, and other Luzhuang areas, successively offering new low prices. For example, the price of Tunxi goods was reduced to 95 yuan, the price of Suian goods was reduced to 80 yuan, and the price of Wuyuan East Road goods was reduced to 102 yuan. The market prices of other items such as Zhenmei Pearl Tea have also been looking to decrease. The green tea market does not present a good picture. As for Keemun and Ningzhou black teas, although transactions are slightly more active, the sales prices have been falling and not rising.

Predictions for the Piece Goods and Woolen Fabric Market [Differing Opinions, Each with Their Own Reasons]

The scorching heat of summer has caused a lull in the woolen fabric trade in May and June. People in the industry are paying close attention to the new market in the autumn and winter, making mutual predictions. For the same goods, some see a rise in prices, while others predict a fall. For example, at the beginning, the general market was expected to rise, but recently it has been looking flat. The reason is that tariffs have been reduced, exchange rates have improved, and costs have become cheaper. In addition, after checking the spring overcoat materials, many Western clothing shops on this street have stored their inventory. The autumn market business will inevitably decrease. However, if merchants from other ports actively purchase, the market may rise accordingly. However, thin flannels, serge, Huate flannels, and other items are being dumped by Japanese imports, and the market sentiment is difficult to turn around. Herringbone flannels and ordinary 4-5 yuan per yard overcoat fabrics are expected to see a good rise in the market in the second half of the year, as jodhpurs and overcoats have been discarded, and herringbone flannels are becoming popular (especially the 4-yuan shiny cloth is the most popular and widespread), and there are no Japanese goods woven. The above is just one type of argument in the market and should not be taken as a firm market view.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talk

More on the "Square Scarf" Mentality

— Ah Long

Previously, I saw an article titled "The 'Square Scarf' Mentality" in this newspaper's supplement, which stirred my thoughts. It led me to believe that if our nation were to perish, it would be, to some extent, related to this "square scarf" mentality.

Two years ago, I advocated for a "short clothing" lifestyle, proposing a significant improvement to men's attire. My reasoning was that since the Xinhai Revolution, there had been much talk about national benefits and people's welfare, but apart from cutting off queues, which indeed benefited the people, I saw little else that could be called national benefits and people's welfare. This made me think that since the Xinhai Revolution, women's clothing had undergone countless changes, becoming bizarre and extravagant, reaching the pinnacle of fashionable transformation (though excessively so). In contrast, men's attire still followed the old style of the Qing Dynasty, remaining unchanged (which was too conservative). Therefore, to awaken the national spirit and promote a simple life, we should first reform the clothing system. At the time, many people advocated for a style similar to Sun Yat-sen's student uniform, knee-length, and entirely made with Chinese tailoring methods. Its advantages were threefold: (1) convenient for walking, (2) saves fabric, and (3) avoids the inconvenience of dragging through mud and water in rain or snow. However, since its advocacy, many people have expressed support, but no one has actually implemented it. It's all just empty talk, causing a temporary stir, but producing no real effect.

Why is this the case? In a word, it's mostly due to the "square scarf" mentality. They would definitely think that if they changed their attire, they would feel embarrassed and uncomfortable if seen by others. Even they themselves would feel it's a loss of gentlemanly decorum. Wearing short clothes, they would feel unable to leave the house, and others would certainly say they are low-class and undignified. What kind of psychology is this? It's the "square scarf" mentality.

In ancient times, dissenting speech was prohibited, and dissenting clothing was punished. Today, we live in a world that values clothing over people. Long gowns and robes are considered dignified and precious. Therefore, even though scholars of the past constantly said "the scholar's hat has misled me," they ultimately refused to discard it. Today, look at those fortune-tellers and geomancers; no matter how tattered and dirty their long gowns and robes are, they would never remove that "square scarf" long gown. Even if a comrade in a long gown falls into dire straits, begging on the roadside, they would still stubbornly refuse to take off their long gown.

Why are they unwilling to take off these clothes? Because I am a superior person, I am a scholar, I am a respectable person. If I wear short clothes, I would lose my status and become a lower-class person. It's a kind of muddled concept of "starving to death is a small matter, but losing propriety is a grave one." I ask again, is the distinction between superior and lower classes really based on long or short clothing? If you are a person without character, no matter how beautiful or authentic your clothes are, you are still "lowly." But if you are a person with character, wearing short clothes wouldn't detract from your dignity. Furthermore, in this era of pragmatism, everything values practicality and eschews formalism. Why wear cumbersome long gowns and robes instead of convenient and fabric-saving clothes? Does removing a long gown really lead to a loss of status? In places like this, some people simply refuse to change. What else can be done?

Recently, Hitler in Germany issued eugenics laws, encouraging marriage and castrating those who are physically weak or have serious illnesses. His plan is solely for the purpose of strengthening the race. The reason why our country is not thriving is that there are too many friends with the "nose-wiping" and "square scarf" mentality. They are mostly thin, pale, weak scholars, mostly domestically produced. They are like the "young male leads" in dramas, wriggling and cringing, making people uncomfortable to watch. If our country is full of such people, even if other countries don't destroy us, we will destroy ourselves.

In the past, Columbus was willing to break an egg to discover a new continent. If the people of our country, in the current environment, don't break down these stubborn habits and class concepts, there is no hope for salvation. However, I also have a statement to make: simply taking off long clothes and putting on short clothes won't strengthen the nation or the body. We must refresh and revitalize all kinds of endeavors like clothing to have any hope of salvation. Otherwise, no matter how much the style of clothing changes, if the attitude of "nose-wiping" and "square scarf" mentality remains unchanged, it won't help.

Page 20

More on Crèches and Public Education

— Shi Shi

(3) Can public education truly benefit children? This is a fundamental question. A parent's love is the sustenance of a child's life. This theoretical point has been discussed in detail in the previous article. However, when we observe the facts, we see that when children are taken away from their families and placed in public education institutions, the result is "the extinction of vitality and the degradation of natural instincts," harming both their physical and mental well-being. The mortality rate of children in Moscow's public education system that I cited earlier is based on the Englishman Hamilton's new book (Memories of Soviet Russia, 1931 edition, distributed by [unclear text]). If Mr. Jiu doubts this, it seems rash. In fact, such examples are too numerous to list. For example, in the book Sociology and Modern Social Problems by the famous American sociologist Charles Ellwood, the mortality rate of children in Paris' public education system is three to four times higher than that of ordinary children. This book is essential reading for those studying social sciences and women's issues and should be even more credible and reliable. Furthermore, the impact on children's spirits and personalities when they leave their families is particularly alarming. According to a 1909 report from 34 government-run juvenile reformatories in the United States, 29 percent of the recalcitrant children admitted were from divorced parents, 32 percent were from incomplete families, and 37 percent were from parents who had committed crimes. Most of these children were abandoned by their parents at a young age and had no home to return to. Conversely, in happy families with both parents, child criminals accounted for less than 1 percent. Furthermore, according to a survey by the Bosted Reformatory in England, more than 90 percent of the residents were homeless orphans. Most surprisingly, children from foster homes and poor children's homes also accounted for more than 27 percent. This shows how important family life and parental education are to children. It is easy to imagine whether public education benefits children.

As for crèches organized under the principle of "public education for children," only the Soviet Union has them at present. Their crèches do not "substitute for parental care" but only provide "foster care." They take "mothers feeding their own children" as a necessary condition and, strictly speaking, do not conform to the original purpose of "public education." In European and American countries, most of them are substitute childcare facilities established under the protection of religious groups and have a charitable nature, which are actually just improved infant homes. I don't know what Mr. Jiu's so-called "reality" is based on. Recently, there has been a labor crèche in our city, which I do not oppose. I remember that the "Rites of Zhou" records: "The Grand Steward uses care and nourishment to nurture all the people, and one day he will care for the young." During the Yuanhe period of the Tang Dynasty, an edict was issued: "Infants without relatives or those who have children but cannot afford to raise them will be provided for." The substitute childcare institutions created under this purpose are, of course, worthy of praise.

Glimpses of July 14th

— Xiao Ying

In the past two days, a common feeling has been revealed on people's faces. The noble people would not have any different feelings, but the working people would!

It's really disappointing to learn from the widespread rumors that there is no hope for this year's "Lantern Festival" again. However, there's no need to mind it; there will always be some excitement.

If you have time to go to the mysterious streets with exotic flavors after the lights are turned on, you will be able to get some stimulation. The pace will naturally be different; the hurried pace shows urgency, the slow pace shows leisure, and the unhurried pace symbolizes the harmony of their mood! As for the posture, of course, it will not be the same either; calm, gentle, inclined... in short, it is countless.

Cars should also come to respond to this great opportunity; convertibles, sedans, sports cars... here, it is not limited to being shiny and bright; even if you drive a dilapidated old car, following the back of the large team will attract attention.

Look, the bright red torches have lost their usual authority, silently hiding in front of the store door, gasping for breath. In the store, the goods are linked together and stitched into very small national emblems and flags, fluttering in front of the house and in the waist of the tree.

Outside the A.K. Soda Fountain, several blue-eyed women are talking and laughing, eating cold drinks, and an intoxicating fragrance blows over, and the working people are stunned.

It's very difficult to squeeze onto the tram, and the heat flow of people is spreading. I guess everyone feels a little distressed? Many people are sighing.

Oh, what's the matter? What's so good about foreign lights? Haven't you seen enough of your own lights at home? the ticket seller said impatiently.

Indeed, what's so good about foreign lights? How do you feel after seeing them? Oh, don't think so much! Now is the time to evolve into a great harmony. If you don't go to see them, it would be really disappointing to build so many lanterns.

The tram doesn't move forward as smoothly as usual; it stops after only a few steps, which is very annoying. The short section of the Eight Immortals Bridge will take 45 minutes. Needless to say, the crowd is even more crowded under the archway lights.

That's right, today the French Park is very lively, but after all, it's a French park! However, in any case, it has a kind of power, attacking everyone's heart. Here, I also went in.

The red and green lights flashing on the trees and in the center of the road are like stars, squeezing their eyes everywhere. The grass is full of people, men, women, and even crying children. On the sidewalks, the crowd is surging like tides. Hey, look! China's population is really prosperous, so prosperous that it can destroy all the construction projects being built in the park and make the neat flowers and trees a mess. This is only a fraction of what's happening in Shanghai!

Leaving the side door, a gust of hot wind swept over, which was very stuffy. Looking to the north, a red light was dyed half the sky.

Whip Marks

— Jenny

Standing painfully in front of the tap, touching the many purple-red whip marks on her arm!

This was just whipped by the master with that leather whip. But when he thought of the leather whip, his nerves suddenly jumped in fright, as if the leather whip was still whipping him; at the same time, the original purple-red whip marks felt faintly painful.

He still didn't know why he was so cruelly whipped by the master with a leather whip. In fact, he didn't think he had done anything wrong today to deserve such a heavy punishment! And he has always been diligent and organized in his work, and no one has ever hated him!

He is an apprentice in the × Barber Shop! Being an apprentice is simply being a vent for the master!

His father is a chauffeur in a mansion, and his family lives in the Yangshupu area. His mother works as a female worker in the nearby × factory. Because the wages that the two of them earn from their sweat and blood cannot maintain the bread for the whole family, they have to entrust relatives and friends to recommend their son to the × Barber Shop as an apprentice!

Naturally, parents know how much their son suffers from the master, but what's the use of knowing? Although it's painful, at least he won't go hungry for three meals a day!

Therefore, although he was whipped by the master's leather whip today, he felt that it was ten thousand times better than being hungry, because in the year before he entered this barber shop, he had been hungry for two days before he could eat a big cake. However, this pain is really unbearable! He instinctively looked at the whip marks on his arm!

Suddenly, the master ran out, still with a stern face, stood in front of him, and nagged: "What are you doing standing here all the time? Do you want to be whipped again? Go sweep the hair on the floor outside clean! Are you still not leaving?..."

So he lowered the two arms full of purple-red whip marks, left the tap, and mechanically ran outside.

Pulling

— Xi Zhen

On a noon of more than 100 degrees, the sun softened the asphalt on the road, and I walked across the street in a hurry.

The asphalt on the street was soft. When the traffic light turned green with the whistle in the patrolman's mouth, the stagnation of cars and people began to move hurriedly and foolishly. Following behind a large string of cars, I saw many people pulling a large truck loaded with many steel bars with all their might. The people pulling were bare-chested, and their skin should have been dark brown. However, under the flames of the sun in this iron smelter, they sweated, and there was no chance to wipe it off. Their bodies were drenched with water, and shone like metal under the sun. Using force, using force! Isn't this tension of bronze muscles a manifestation of strength? Pulling the rope, the rope as thick as a carrying pole was wrapped around the shoulders, and as they pulled, it half sank into the flesh. A deep groove was carved out of the shoulders and back. Several people, all like that, leaned forward with all their might, forming an acute angle with the ground, desperately, and looking at the green light of the traffic light, anxiously fearing that it would turn red and they would not be able to cross the street. In this way, everyone looked at each other (agreeing), each person)

Page 21

shouting "Pull!" "Pull!" from their mouths, and the clumsy truck moved foolishly.

An impression flashed like lightning: "What a difficult struggle for survival!"

Forgetting the heat of the sun, I stood in the hot sun, watching them struggle across the street in the green light of the traffic light.

And the cars on the street were still moving foolishly, but I felt as if I was pulling some clumsy thing, feeling a kind of weight, a kind of force, hanging behind me. But just like that, I desperately pulled my own life and walked many difficult roads from the dangerous and boiling road. Undoubtedly, I am still running on a difficult road, and when this difficulty falls on our generation, I am afraid that the face of the future reality will make us even more afraid. However, what does it matter? Let the burden behind us increase as much weight as possible, let the road become more boiling, more steep, and more dark; when the instinct of survival is pushing us from behind, and the purpose of survival is pulling us from the front, what does the steepness of the road and the hardship of labor matter to us?

Looking at the coolies pulling the cart, the manifestation of strength enlightened me. Every struggle is not a pleasant thing, but when suffering, they know to shout "Pull!" (agreeing) to the people who are standing on the same direction and pulling each other, and this shout, among them, will undoubtedly be a kind of permission for common cooperation and comfort for mutual assistance. They keep shouting and clamoring on the road; and I understand that because of this mutual permission and comfort, they have the courage to step on difficult steps.

Amateur Mailbox

Can a Vocation Provide a Living?

Mr. Editor:

Women are pitiful! Especially the semi-new and semi-old Chinese women! After my parents died, I have two younger brothers and one younger sister. My family is naturally poor, but I don't need to say that. I just want to talk about my own problems and ask for your guidance.

I am twenty-one years old this year! I have studied in junior high school, high school, and private school; but I don't have a graduation diploma. Shackled by qualifications, I can't find anything to do. As a last resort, in this environment, I worked as a shop assistant for half a year, living a life of selling my face, so to speak. This kind of job will definitely not be stable when I get older. People like me who are melancholy and sick are getting old very quickly. Therefore, I should plan for my lifelong plan:

It just so happened that a gentleman often came to the store to buy things. From acquaintance to acquaintance, he became acquainted with me. He is very good to me, two years older than me. He graduated from a domestic university and works in an agency. His monthly salary can be more than a hundred yuan. He is very interested in marrying me, and even swore an oath of love to me, saying that he would never abandon me. But later, when he talked about him being already married, I fainted to the ground and was at a loss!

He said: "He will definitely not let me down, but how can the crime of bigamy be good?" I become his concubine, and there is no such provision in law. I am not very willing to be a mistress! That's even worse! Therefore, I ended up with no home to return to and no way to go! He finally comforted me and said, "He is from Guangdong and is about to return to Southeast Asia. If he goes to the United States, he will get a master's degree in one year and will definitely marry me when he comes back." Now my living expenses are all supplied by him, because when I was very passionate with him, the store was abandoned and I was fired. He wants me to go back to school and set a two-year deadline to learn a vocation that can support myself. I think about it again and again, can a vocation provide a living? Can I succeed in two years? Calling me to make a living on my own must mean that I am breaking off relations with me; or that I am still connected. But living this kind of shameless life, what is the joy of being born into the world? When I bring up the marriage issue again, he and his wife have feelings that cannot be divorced. I absolutely refuse to be the kind of unvirtuous woman who steals love. "One wrong step will cause eternal regret." I can't marry, I can't recruit, and there are really many differences between pitiful women and men. Freedom is what we all sacrifice our lives to demand, and freedom is also the path to our depravity. I am afraid that my problem can only be solved by the tracks on the railway and the long flow of the Huangpu River! But maybe the gentleman has a better way, so please teach me and let me follow. I am really very grateful. Best wishes for

good health! Chen Yonglian bows

Answer: I carefully read your letter and feel that you still regard marriage as entering a "sustenance institute," where both material and spiritual life must be resolved through marriage. There are indeed many people who hold this kind of "parasitic" mentality. It's no wonder you feel that way. Under the current social relations, women are forced to be parasites. However, because of this, you feel that your "lifelong plan" cannot be arranged, and that "only the tracks on the railway and the long flow of the Huangpu River" can solve the problem for you. In fact, your experience, although pitiful, is not necessarily a dead end. As long as you have the courage and independent spirit to do things, your problem is very easy to solve.

Although that college student's association with you may not have pure intentions, it is inevitable that he has a bit of a psychology of playing with women and seeking his own carnal satisfaction. Now, maybe he really wants to "break off relations" with you, but he still hopes that you will spend two years to learn a vocation that can support yourself. He is not as conscienceless as others. In other words, you have not met a liar, and your life has not been ruined in his hands. In my opinion, the reason for your distress is that you have underestimated yourself too much, so you have the questions "Can a vocation provide a living?" "Can I succeed in two years?" It seems that women cannot live without relying on their husbands. You must thoroughly eliminate this slave mentality, otherwise, even if you truly get what you call a home, you will only be a slave to others for the rest of your life. Although you have not obtained a formal diploma from school, you already have a high school education. Judging from this letter, your handwriting is very clear and neat, and your sentences are fluent and coherent. Even sloppy college graduates may not be able to catch up with you. Therefore, you are not a person without any foundation. If you have two more years to study, I guarantee that you can learn a specialized skill. Therefore, you are not afraid of not finding the qualification for a "able to live" vocation. I think the center of the problem is that you have to be reliable in doing things. Although he now allows you two years to study, I don't know if he can give you the tuition and living expenses for these two years. If not, you must ask him to give it to you all at once to avoid him changing his mind halfway. This is the most important thing.

Of course, the purpose of a woman marrying a husband, although now everyone thinks it is for "eating," is actually not so simple. Family life and desire for a spouse are human nature. However, the problem that most people cannot marry is still caused by economic reasons. If the economic problem is solved, there will be far fewer difficulties. If you are economically independent, it will be much easier for you to marry. Now, most wage earners hope to get a wife who does not have to bear economic responsibility. Even if you are very good to that college student, and you don't want anyone else, you can continue to maintain the relationship. Under the current circumstances, you must go through the marriage form to maintain it, but at that time, it is not necessary. The love between two people does not have to go through the marriage form to be maintained. Therefore, you are not a desperate person in terms of sexual life.

Your problem is not a problem. What has become a problem is that you don't want to treat yourself as a person and regard yourself as a parasite. Editor

Novel

Revenge (2)

— Translated from Hungarian by Youlibakiluo Jia

A four-wheeled carriage stopped at the gate of a street house. The mother was the first to get out and waited for her daughter. But the daughter remained motionless, as if she had no intention of following.

"We're home," the mother said in surprise.

"Good! I know: : : Go to sleep!"

"Welcome!"

To make the coachman not understand their conversation, the young lady said in French:

"Tomorrow is already the wedding day. I obey you, but today I am still free, and I still have to dispose of myself at will."

"What do you want to do?"

"I want to avenge myself: : : I want to come up with a true woman's revenge: : :"

The mother stared at her daughter in terror, guessing at that terrible result, and she cried out:

"You're crazy. What do you want to do?"

The young lady laughed, painfully but almost threateningly, said:

"I will tell you in the future: ...No, don't be afraid. I won't commit suicide, and I won't hinder the restoration of the basis of the property of my parents' enterprise. I just want to avenge myself: : :".

"But it's so late, where are you going? : : : You're crazy, you're completely crazy."

Instead of answering, the young lady gave the coachman an order:

"Hey, go back to the dance floor!"

The national carriage began to run. The mother desperately shouted, trying to stop them, but the young lady kept giving orders to the coachman.

"If you take me to Hilda Street very quickly, I can give you a lot of tip money."

"Not to the dance hall?"

"No! To Hilda Street! Do you understand?"

"Yes!"

The young lady opened the small window of the car and looked at her mother, who was following the car that had started running. The young lady mischievously protruded:

"Dear mother, don't run! I'll be home in an hour."

The wheels resounded on the street stones, and their voices drowned out the mother's reply.

Film Special

The Audience's Policy of Burying Their Heads in the Sand and the Masks Worn by Celebrities (Part 1)

— Su Yin

American President Lincoln once said: "You cannot fool all of the people all of the time." This saying is mostly correct, but he didn't thoroughly understand human psychology. He didn't investigate how many people in the world are constantly trying to fool themselves, or deliberately asking others to fool them. If you awaken these people from their dreams or expose their illusions, they will grieve and mourn. There are no statistics on exactly how many such people there are in the world, but some people boldly say that all the gentlemen and ladies, just because they have a bit of money, are willing to buy pink-tinted glasses to wear. Emptiness, fantasy, and splendor are ways to escape reality. Although Soviet writers strive to depict reality, the masses still prefer to see the best, hear the best, and believe the best—even if those things aren't entirely true—especially about the idols they worship.

How mysterious is Greta Garbo, and how did she become so mysterious? It's actually quite funny. According to her confidants, on her first day in America, reporters came to see her, but because of the language barrier, she couldn't say a word, so she simply kept silent. They felt that this Swedish girl was extraordinary, so they gave her the title of "Mysterious Girl." This title was worth its weight in gold, and Greta soon realized it from her bank account. So she became even more mysterious. The audience, too, felt that the more mysterious she was, the better, so Greta had to maintain her mystery, because her position was built on this empty fantasy. Is Garbo really mysterious? I'm afraid there's more mystery in a beef patty. Now, if what's published in film magazines isn't mysterious enough, her fans will fill in the gaps with their submissions. The easiest way to incur public opposition is to declare that Garbo is no different from anyone else. She keeps one eye on the public's infatuation with her inexplicable mystery and the other on the booming ticket sales, secretly delighted.

Regarding the marital events of general celebrities, the public often harbors many fabricated fantasies about them. Take Ann Harding, for example. Since her divorce from her husband, Harry Bannister, her status has been greatly affected. This is because her previous publicity always mentioned how happy their marriage was, how they would grow old together, and how they were role models for all of Hollywood, etc. Of course, when the marriage later broke down and the truth was revealed, it was the day the illusions of her fans, especially housewives, were shattered. The divorce of Janet Gaynor and Lydell Peck was similar. Previously, everyone regarded Janet as a sweet, approachable girl. Then they all realized that Janet also had strange and stubborn sides. Therefore, her status was also significantly affected. Fortunately, she had a few good films that maintained her connection with the audience. However, it wasn't the general public who knew about Janet's various faults, but rather the Hollywood authorities. Not long ago, we heard news that a certain luminary in the film industry was about to divorce. We thought that since we were insiders, it would be fine to discuss the details with close friends. Who knew that after hearing the real story, they wouldn't even say thank you, but instead accused us of spreading rumors. One very clever bystander said, "Please don't talk about that kind of thing. I prefer to keep that fantasy intact, so it will never disappear, because that is the only way for me to escape the cruel reality." This is how the public prefers to bury their heads in the sand and avoid reality. (To be continued)

Film Reviews

Review of "King of the Wild Horses"

— Wan Shi

"King of the Wild Horses" | Carleton

This is a film starring a horse.

Originally, this shouldn't be a strange thing. When a horse that can act is discovered, it's as if finding a dog that can act. The producers can regard it as a rare treasure, because they can use it to exploit the audience's curiosity. Rin Tin Tin or Tom Mix's horse—weren't they all once clever animals that caused a sensation?

Human bodies have already become commodities, let alone animals?

It is precisely because of this horse named Rex, precisely because this horse has amazing skills, that screenwriters, directors, and photographers are mobilized for this horse, and even many actors are directed to play supporting roles for it. Everything is very simple; everything is for a horse.

If you think that the impostor official's exploitation of the people is an exposure of the poor local political organization, then it is unreasonable and exaggerated. Western films often have this kind of plot.

We won't gain any new understanding from it. All we see are the horse's jumps and the bravery of the chief's son. As for film art, that's out of the question here.

Audience Opinions

Review of "Fallen Souls"

— Yu Hong

"Fallen Souls" is the latest work of the Yueming Company. Although the content is still so immature and unable to satisfy us, in terms of form, there is indeed a lot of progress. This is a point that we should encourage in a small company.

Originally, amidst this socio-economic destruction, the instability of workers' lives has long become an undeniable fact. However, the reason for the instability of workers' lives belongs to the serious problems of the entire social organization, and is definitely not the demon (woman) who harms the soul as pointed out by the director. Although women are sometimes a kind of destruction of human life, the director here fails to point out the major reasons for the bankruptcy of workers' lives, and only uses a woman to represent everything, which is also suspected of avoiding the important and dwelling on the trivial. At the same time, because the consciousness is inaccurate, there is naturally little powerful development in the plot. The overall impression given to the audience is nothing more than "women are not good things"!

The director's control skills are also insufficient, such as Mina's sudden arrival with boxes and no detailed introduction, such as Hu's wife moving and not informing Hu Fei in prison, and necessarily meeting after buying cakes, and many other loopholes. But there are also some very exciting places, such as the scene of Xiao Fei's storm during illness, which is very realistic. Especially using a broken umbrella in a leaky house, and writing back the dance umbrella in the ballroom, and using coffee in the ballroom to reflect Hu's wife's drinking roadside tea, these are all good techniques and worthy of praise. However, the darkness of the light is indeed the biggest stain on this film! (Omitted below)

Watching "Fallen Souls"

— Hou Yimin

"Fallen Souls" depicts the romantic history of a courtesan. Indeed, in the story, it depicts the evils of the city, the extravagance, and everything else without reservation. It tells us that the city is so evil, and directs us to be safe and secure, right? Don't have any unrealistic ideas, otherwise, you will go astray, and you don't know what to do!

However, the writing of the script is too messy and too scattered. There is never a scene that can grab the audience's psychology and be extremely tense, but just a series of bland performances. As for the director's directing skills, it seems that it is not enough, so the performance of the whole play has no place for change, and it is always a series of the same shots.

Because most of the exteriors, such as the city and the countryside, are taken in the Shanghai area, the scenery is very economical, and there is not much scenery to be used. However, what disappoints us is that the scenery of several interior scenes seems to be too sloppy, and even has many illogical places.

The actors' performances are mediocre, and there is nothing outstanding. Because the plot is scattered, and the central characters in the play are scattered, it makes it impossible for everyone to perform fully. Comparatively speaking, it is Wang Feijuan, who plays Hu Fei's wife, and her performance is more profound. Generally speaking, the production of a small company, "Fallen Souls", can be said to be a domestic film at the horizontal level!

Francis Ton's Romance

— Dong Lin

Up to now, Francis Ton has been in love twice. He has been engaged to his second partner for several years. However, because she is a very promising actress, if they get married, it will undoubtedly destroy her bright future, so he has to endure it, planning for her future, and separating from her.

Since this sad anecdote became known, Francis Ton has greatly gained sympathy from all sides, and his reputation has also increased because of this.

The identity of the female partner who has become a problem is still kept secret and not made public. But many people say that it is probably Sylvia Sidney.

Liliane Hawe's "Emerging Lotus"

— Shen Weng

This film "Emerging Lotus" [Love Never Again] uses satirical techniques to discuss the issue of male lust.

A group of men who have been wronged by women are really tired of beauty. With temporary courage, they ran to the sea together and vowed not to get close to the opposite sex anymore. At first, everyone sang the song "Farewell to Love" with a 12-point determination, but as the days passed, everyone gradually felt sexually hungry, so they often had fantasies, and one by one they were about to become crazy. At this time, by chance, they suddenly discovered a stunning beauty in a bathrobe on the sea. This delicate and tender emerging lotus, when seen by those men who crave women day and night, how could they not be moved? There's no need for me to go on about what happened next.

This film stars Liliane Hawe and is scheduled to be publicly screened at the Nanjing Grand Theater in this city on the 18th (Wednesday).

Silver Screen Gossip

— Bai Pin

Regardless of whether "sacrificing for art" is true or false, film critics should always forgive them. They often see in film reviews the subjective statement "××× does not hesitate to sacrifice her body for people:::" This is inappropriate, because although she has the right to "not want" to film a sensual scene (and only a few actresses can do so), the screenwriter and director are responsible. They are just pitiful people who are "powerless to resist"!

Of course, "sensual films" are not what the times need, and criticism is justified, but don't mistakenly knock the puppet's head. The accounting should be settled with the "behind-the-scenes people."

Film Novel

Thirty-Day Princess (5)

— Jin Que

Not only Spotswood and two policemen went to visit Mrs. Smith, but also many reporters followed. One of them, named Gilchrist, was a reporter from the Madison newspaper. When they followed there, Mrs. Smith told them that Nancy had been missing for several days. Gilchrist was a very shrewd reporter. He found a photo of Nancy in Nancy's house and showed it to Mrs. Smith, proving that it was Nancy herself. So he rushed back to his newspaper, convinced that he had received a unique and amazing message. "It turns out that Princess Catalina is not a princess at all," he told Madison. "The one in Grächen is a missing Nancy. She is an actress who is now impersonating a princess to help Grächen issue bonds!" Madison was still half-believing, and did not dare to fully agree. However, he also admitted that the photo that Gilchrist took was indeed very similar to Catalina. Later, he said to Gilchrist: "But I personally know the princess. Also, the princess came by boat, right?" Gilchrist said: "Although the princess came by boat, like before, she can also enter the quarantine island and not be able to land." So they discussed a discounted method. They first published a piece of news about Nancy's disappearance, and published a photo of her and a photo of a makeup box she had left in a nightclub the night before. They also drafted a news headline, vaguely pointing to many shady scenes and kidnapping situations inside. Madison also promised Gilchrist to try his best to prove that Princess Katherina was not a princess at all, but Nancy.

When the news was published the next day, and there was a photo of the princess's makeup life box, saying that it was Nancy's, Madison himself passed out several times. But he also had no way to think about it. That kind of nightclub fight::: actually involved the princess's Qingming::: it was really an incredible thing. Grächen was so angry that his face turned purple when he saw the news. He condemned Nancy, saying that she disregarded her position, had an affair with Madison privately, and ran into nightclubs with him, endangering all the tasks, and was also careless with the princess's private property, arbitrarily leaving it outside. But the matter was already so, and there was no way to recover it. So they decided to go on a trip to avoid the limelight for a while. Madison heard that the princess was going out for a trip, of course, he was reluctant and heartbroken, but when he went to the station to see her off, he suffered an unexpected pain. Because when the train was about to leave, a Duke Nicholas rushed to the station. Madison inquired that the Duke Nicholas was the princess's fiancé. Nicholas wanted to go out for a trip with the princess, but the princess didn't want him to go. They argued. Grächen was also not convenient to force Nancy. He also knew that Nicholas's mouth was very loose. He was afraid that going together would be detrimental to his plan. At this time, Gilchrist was also at the station. When he saw the dispute between Nicholas and the princess, he immediately surrounded Nicholas. He asked Nicholas many questions, trying to find out some real content, but he intentionally or unintentionally made Nicholas believe that the princess had changed, or that the princess was not the former princess, and it was not known.
